vertical-align: baseline;">Google-managed Model Context Protocol (MCP) servers</span></a><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> are generally available or in preview, with more on the way.</span></p> <p><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Why it matters:</strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> To move beyond experimental prototypes, AI agents must be able to access real-world data and solve complex problems autonomously.</span></p> <p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">Google-managed Managed Context Protocol (MCP) servers provide the critical connectivity to bridge AI agents with the vast Google and Google Cloud ecosystems. By hosting these servers on an enterprise-ready, standardized platform, we eliminate the need to integrate with local MCP servers and offer a unified developer experience that’s integrated across major agent runtimes and frameworks.</span></p> <h3><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">MCP built for the enterprise</span></h3></div> <div class="block-image_full_width"> <div class="article-module h-c-page"> <div class="h-c-grid"> <figure class="article-image--large h-c-grid__col h-c-grid__col--6 h-c-grid__col--offset-3 " > <img src="https://storage.googleapis.com/gweb-cloudblog-publish/images/1_nAhagkS.max-1000x1000.png" alt="1"> </a> </figure> </div> </div> </div> <div class="block-paragraph_advanced"><p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">Scaling your agent ecosystem shouldn't be a trade-off between speed and safety. You need the flexibility to grow, but you also need the guardrails to manage and govern your agents.</span></p> <p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">By pointing your AI agents toward Google-managed MCP endpoints, you’re plugging into the Google Cloud security stack, without needing to make regional configuration changes . While the platform offers deep flexibility for a range of architectures, here’s a snapshot of their capabilities that make it easier:</span></p> <ul> <li aria-level="1" style="list-style-type: disc; vertical-align: baseline;"> <p role="presentation"><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Strong interoperability: </strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">Through protocol translation, your agents stay compliant with the </span><a href="https://modelcontextprotocol.io/specification/" rel="noopener" target="_blank"><span style="text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">MCP specification</span></a><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">, so that they play nice with public agents and agent frameworks like Gemini CLI, Claude, ChatGPT, VS Code, LangChain, Agent Development Kit (ADK), and CrewAI right out of the box. For example, we added support for </span><a href="https://modelcontextprotocol.io/specification/2025-11-25/server" rel="noopener" target="_blank"><span style="text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">Resources and Prompts</span></a><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> as primitives in the MCP protocol in addition to Tools.</span></p> </li> <li aria-level="1" style="list-style-type: disc; vertical-align: baseline;"> <p role="presentation"><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Centralized discovery:</strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> No more hunting for MCP servers and tools. </span><a href="https://docs.cloud.google.com/agent-registry/overview"><span style="text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">Agent Registry</span></a><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> offers a unified directory where you can easily find and manage agents, MCP servers, and tools in one place.</span></p> </li> <li aria-level="1" style="list-style-type: disc; vertical-align: baseline;"> <p role="presentation"><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Easy access with security and governance: </strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">Every Google Cloud service is now MCP-enabled by default, allowing agents to easily communicate with Google Cloud. Leverage native </span><a href="https://docs.cloud.google.com/mcp/control-mcp-use-iam#deny-all-mcp-tool-use"><span style="text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">Cloud IAM</span></a><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> Deny policy for fine-grained access control. </span></p> </li> <li aria-level="1" style="list-style-type: disc; vertical-align: baseline;"> <p role="presentation"><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Content safety: </strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">With </span><a href="https://docs.cloud.google.com/model-armor/model-armor-mcp-google-cloud-integration"><span style="text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">Model Armor</span></a><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> in-line integration, you can actively defend against indirect prompt injections and data exfiltration.</span></p> </li> <li aria-level="1" style="list-style-type: disc; vertical-align: baseline;"> <p role="presentation"><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Full observability:</strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> Maintain full oversight with OTel Tracing and </span><a href="https://docs.cloud.google.com/logging/docs/audit"><span style="text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">Cloud Audit Logs</span></a><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">, helping you troubleshoot your agents, get comprehensive analytics, and perform forensic audits of agentic actions.</span></p> </li> </ul> <h3><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">Case study: Insta360 redefines video editing</span></h3> <p><a href="https://www.insta360.com/" rel="noopener" target="_blank"><span style="text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">Insta360</span></a><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">, one of the world’s leading smart imaging brands, is leveraging the Google Cloud agentic ecosystem to redefine how users capture and share their lives. Building on its "Moments" feature, which delivers AI video highlights, the company developed an AI video editing agent using Google's Agent Development Kit, Agent Engine, A2A and Google-managed MCP servers, allowing users to complete video editing in the cloud through natural language input.</span></p></div> <div class="block-video"> <div class="article-module article-video "> <figure> <a class="h-c-video h-c-video--marquee" href="https://youtube.com/watch?v=oZTRT0PnbEc" data-glue-modal-trigger="uni-modal-oZTRT0PnbEc-" data-glue-modal-disabled-on-mobile="true"> <div class="article-video__aspect-image" style="background-image: url(https://storage.googleapis.com/gweb-cloudblog-publish/images/maxresdefault_bZxNlFf.max-1000x1000.jpg);"> <span class="h-u-visually-hidden">Insta360</span> </div> <svg role="img" class="h-c-video__play h-c-icon h-c-icon--color-white"> <use xlink:href="#mi-youtube-icon"></use> </svg> </a> </figure> </div> <div class="h-c-modal--video" data-glue-modal="uni-modal-oZTRT0PnbEc-" data-glue-modal-close-label="Close Dialog"> <a class="glue-yt-video" data-glue-yt-video-autoplay="true" data-glue-yt-video-height="99%" data-glue-yt-video-vid="oZTRT0PnbEc" data-glue-yt-video-width="100%" href="https://youtube.com/watch?v=oZTRT0PnbEc" ng-cloak> </a> </div> </div> <div class="block-paragraph_advanced"><p style="padding-left: 40px;"><span style="font-style: italic; vertical-align: baseline;">“Transitioning to managed MCP servers will allow us to move away from fragile point-to-point connections and toward a secure, scalable service-oriented architecture. By exposing our proprietary editing tools as managed endpoints, we're gaining the enterprise-grade stability needed to bring autonomous video creation to users around the world.</span><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">” - Even Lin, Head of Cloud Services, Insta360</span></p> <h3><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">Broad coverage across the Google ecosystem</span></h3></div> <div class="block-image_full_width"> <div class="article-module h-c-page"> <div class="h-c-grid"> <figure class="article-image--large h-c-grid__col h-c-grid__col--6 h-c-grid__col--offset-3 " > <img src="https://storage.googleapis.com/gweb-cloudblog-publish/images/2_v1J3DSa.max-1000x1000.png" alt="2"> </a> </figure> </div> </div> </div> <div class="block-paragraph_advanced"><p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">Whether you’re automating internal operations or building customer-facing experiences, Google-managed MCP servers let your models do more than just chat; they provide the secure connections needed to take direct action across your Google Cloud services. Here are a few ways you can leverage them today:</span></p> <h3><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">1. Infrastructure, operations, and security</strong></h3> <p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">Agents can help move beyond simple monitoring to active orchestration, handling maintenance and monitoring while prioritizing critical security events. Here are a few examples of what this looks like in practice: </span></p> <ul> <li aria-level="1" style="list-style-type: disc; vertical-align: baseline;"> <p role="presentation"><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Automated lifecycle management (ALM):</strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> Provision and decommission resources dynamically based on real-time application demand using </span><a href="https://docs.cloud.google.com/kubernetes-engine/docs/reference/mcp"><span style="text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">GKE</span></a><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">, </span><a href="https://docs.cloud.google.com/run/docs/reference/mcp"><span style="text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">Cloud Run</span></a><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">, or </span><a href="https://docs.cloud.google.com/compute/docs/reference/mcp"><span style="text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">GCE</span></a><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> MCP servers.</span></p> </li> <li aria-level="1" style="list-style-type: disc; vertical-align: baseline;"> <p role="presentation"><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Self-healing systems: </strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">Empower agents to monitor events via </span><a href="https://docs.cloud.google.com/logging/docs/reference/v2_mcp/mcp"><span style="text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">Cloud Logging</span></a><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> and </span><a href="https://docs.cloud.google.com/monitoring/api/ref_v3_mcp/mcp"><span style="text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">Monitoring</span></a><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">, triggering recovery actions like traffic rerouting or deployment rollbacks before users are impacted.</span></p> </li> <li aria-level="1" style="list-style-type: disc; vertical-align: baseline;"> <p role="presentation"><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Security orchestration: </strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">Build sophisticated workflows that use </span><a href="https://docs.cloud.google.com/chronicle/docs/reference/mcp"><span style="text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">Google Security Operations</span></a><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> to automatically investigate and respond to emerging threats.</span></p> </li> <li aria-level="1" style="list-style-type: disc; vertical-align: baseline;"> <p role="presentation"><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Fleet and network ops:</strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> Use the </span><a href="https://developers.google.com/android/management/use-android-management-mcp" rel="noopener" target="_blank"><span style="text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">Android Management API</span></a><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> MCP server to query device health in natural language, or utilize </span><a href="https://docs.cloud.google.com/network-intelligence-center/docs/reference/networkmanagement/rest"><span style="text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">Network Management API</span></a><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> MCP server to automate complex diagnostic workflows and surface actionable insights instantly.</span></p> </li> </ul> <h3><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">2. Databases, analytics, and storage</strong></h3> <p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">To be effective, an agent must be grounded in </span><a href="https://cloud.google.com/transform/the-prompt-unlock-ai-agents-with-enterprise-truth?e=48754805"><span style="text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">enterprise truth</span></a><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> — the live, operational data residing in your production systems. This enables agents to interact with your data ecosystem with:</span></p> <ul> <li aria-level="1" style="list-style-type: disc; vertical-align: baseline;"> <p role="presentation"><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Real-time operational insights:</strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> Connect agents directly to </span><a href="https://docs.cloud.google.com/spanner/docs/reference/mcp"><span style="text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">Spanner</span></a><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">, </span><a href="https://docs.cloud.google.com/alloydb/docs/reference/mcp"><span style="text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">AlloyDB</span></a><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">, </span><a href="https://docs.cloud.google.com/sql/docs/mysql/reference/mcp"><span style="text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">Cloud SQL</span></a><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">, </span><a href="https://docs.cloud.google.com/firestore/docs/reference/mcp"><span style="text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">Firestore</span></a><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">, or </span><a href="https://docs.cloud.google.com/bigtable/docs/reference/admin/mcp"><span style="text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">Bigtable</span></a><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> MCP servers to give agents access to both structured and unstructured operational data, to power immediate, data-driven decision-making.</span></p> </li> <li aria-level="1" style="list-style-type: disc; vertical-align: baseline;"> <p role="presentation"><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Analytical insights and data pipelines: </strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">Leverage </span><a href="https://docs.cloud.google.com/bigquery/docs/reference/mcp"><span style="text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">BigQuery</span></a><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> and </span><a href="https://docs.cloud.google.com/dataproc/docs/guides/use-dataproc-mcp"><span style="text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">Managed Service for Apache Spark</span></a><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> MCP servers to process large datasets, using </span><a href="https://docs.cloud.google.com/pubsub/docs/use-pubsub-mcp"><span style="text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">Pub/Sub</span></a><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> or </span><a href="https://docs.cloud.google.com/managed-service-for-apache-kafka/docs/use-managed-service-for-apache-kafka-mcp"><span style="text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">Managed Service for Apache Kafka</span></a><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> to trigger proactive system alerts.</span></p> </li> <li aria-level="1" style="list-style-type: disc; vertical-align: baseline;"> <p role="presentation"><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Contextual retrieval:</strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> Access both structured and unstructured data with </span><a href="https://docs.cloud.google.com/storage/docs/reference/mcp"><span style="text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">Google Cloud Storage</span></a><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> and </span><a href="https://docs.cloud.google.com/dataplex/docs/mcp-overview"><span style="text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">Knowledge Catalog</span></a><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> MCP servers to provide agents with real-time context required to accurately execute complex tasks.</span></p> </li> </ul> <h3><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">3. Services and apps</strong></h3> <p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">Beyond raw data, agents require geographic context, technical documentation, and productivity tools to operate effectively. Here are ways agents can leverage these tools to perform more sophisticated and helpful tasks:</span></p> <ul> <li aria-level="1" style="list-style-type: disc; vertical-align: baseline;"> <p role="presentation"><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Developer assistance:</strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> The </span><a href="https://developers.google.com/knowledge/reference/mcp" rel="noopener" target="_blank"><span style="text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">Developer Knowledge API</span></a><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> MCP server grounds AI agents in Google's official developer documentation, allowing tools to reference up-to-date code samples and guides to solve complex technical issues as they happen.</span></p> </li> <li aria-level="1" style="list-style-type: disc; vertical-align: baseline;"> <p role="presentation"><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Hyper-local contextual intelligence:</strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> Use </span><a href="https://developers.google.com/maps/ai/grounding-lite/reference/mcp" rel="noopener" target="_blank"><span style="text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">Maps Grounding Lite</span></a><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> MCP server to provide agents with trusted Google Maps data. Deliver high-precision responses for routing, weather, and local points of interest, minimizing hallucinations in travel and real-estate applications.</span></p> </li> <li aria-level="1" style="list-style-type: disc; vertical-align: baseline;"> <p role="presentation"><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Conversational experience design:</strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> The </span><a href="https://docs.cloud.google.com/vertex-ai/docs/reference/mcp"><span style="text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">Gemini Enterprise Agent Platform</span></a><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> MCP server empowers agents to act as AI supervisors, programmatically managing the full lifecycle of other models, prompts, and endpoints. Additionally, the </span><a href="https://docs.cloud.google.com/customer-engagement-ai/conversational-agents/ps/mcp-server"><span style="text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">Customer Experience Agent Studio</span></a><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> MCP server enables AI-assisted workflows for building, modifying, and maintaining customer experience agents.</span></p> </li> <li aria-level="1" style="list-style-type: disc; vertical-align: baseline;"> <p role="presentation"><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Productivity and commerce</strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">: Streamline team collaboration with Workspace MCP Servers for </span><a href="https://developers.google.com/workspace/gmail/api/guides/configure-mcp-server" rel="noopener" target="_blank"><span style="text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">Gmail</span></a><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">, </span><a href="https://developers.google.com/workspace/drive/api/guides/configure-mcp-server" rel="noopener" target="_blank"><span style="text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">Drive</span></a><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">, </span><a href="https://developers.google.com/workspace/calendar/api/guides/configure-mcp-server" rel="noopener" target="_blank"><span style="text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">Calendar</span></a><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">, </span><a href="https://developers.google.com/people/v1/configure-mcp-server" rel="noopener" target="_blank"><span style="text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">People API</span></a><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">, and </span><a href="https://developers.google.com/workspace/chat/api/guides/configure-mcp-server" rel="noopener" target="_blank"><span style="text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">Chat</span></a><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> by allowing agents to summarize Gmail threads, draft Docs, manage Calendar invites and facilitate Google Chat workflows to streamline team productivity. Additionally, with </span><a href="https://developers.google.com/pay/api/web/reference/mcp" rel="noopener" target="_blank"><span style="text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">Google Pay and Wallet</span></a><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> MCP server, you can integrate payments and digital passes into your agentic workflows, allowing AI to assist with onboarding, troubleshooting integrations, and monitoring checkout performance.</span></p> </li> </ul> <p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">By unifying these capabilities with MCP, it’s easier than ever to build agents that don't just chat, but actually take actions on your behalf.</span></p> <h3><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Technical scenario with demo</strong></h3></div> <div class="block-image_full_width"> <div class="article-module h-c-page"> <div class="h-c-grid"> <figure class="article-image--large h-c-grid__col h-c-grid__col--6 h-c-grid__col--offset-3 " > <img src="https://storage.googleapis.com/gweb-cloudblog-publish/original_images/3_nnqZkLT.gif" alt="3"> </a> </figure> </div> </div> </div> <div class="block-paragraph_advanced"><p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">To showcase the power of this platform, we built the Pet Passport demo using Google-managed MCP servers and ADK. </span></p> <p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">This demo features an autonomous agent that handles a complete end-to-end workflow: planning the perfect pet-friendly day out in New York City. The agent implements a macro-to-micro reasoning chain:</span></p> <ol> <li aria-level="1" style="list-style-type: decimal; vertical-align: baseline;"> <p role="presentation"><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">First, it uses the BigQuery MCP server to analyze the NYC Dog License dataset and identify the specific neighborhood where a user's dog breed is most popular. </span></p> </li> <li aria-level="1" style="list-style-type: decimal; vertical-align: baseline;"> <p role="presentation"><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">Next, it passes that context to the Google Maps MCP server to generate a verified walking route complete with dog parks and cafes. </span></p> </li> </ol> <p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">When it's time to go live, Gemini CLI leverages the Cloud Run MCP server to deploy the agent application directly from a local machine, publishing the entire experience as a live, shareable URL.</span></p> <p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">Try it yourself with the </span><a href="https://codelabs.developers.google.com/next26/build-adk-agent-google-mcps" rel="noopener" target="_blank"><span style="text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">codelab</span></a><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> or explore the source code on </span><a href="https://github.com/google/mcp/tree/main/examples/petpassport" rel="noopener" target="_blank"><span style="text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">GitHub</span></a><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">.</span></p> <h3><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Start building today </strong></h3> <p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">We invite you to build production-grade workflows using the </span><a href="https://geminicli.com/" rel="noopener" target="_blank"><span style="text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">Gemini CLI</span></a><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">, </span><a href="https://docs.cloud.google.com/gemini-enterprise-agent-platform/build/adk"><span style="text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">ADK</span></a><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">, or your preferred IDE.</span></p></div>Tue, 28 Apr 2026 17:00:00 +0000https://cloud.google.com/blog/products/ai-machine-learning/google-managed-mcp-servers-are-available-for-everyone/AI & Machine Learningarticle50+ fully managed MCP servers now available for Google Cloud servicesGooglehttps://cloud.google.com/blog/products/ai-machine-learning/google-managed-mcp-servers-are-available-for-everyone/Vidya NagarajanDirector of Product Management, Google CloudYubin GongPrincipal Engineer, Google CloudDay 2 at Google Cloud Next: A marathon developer keynotehttps://cloud.google.com/blog/topics/google-cloud-next/next26-day-2-recap/<div class="block-paragraph_advanced"><p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">At Google Cloud, every day is Developer Day, but none so much as day 2 of Google Cloud Next, when we hold the developer keynote.  This year’s topic? An in-depth look at </span><a href="https://cloud.google.com/blog/products/ai-machine-learning/introducing-gemini-enterprise-agent-platform"><span style="text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">Gemini Enterprise Agent Platform</span></a><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">. This year’s theme? Planning a marathon for 10,000 participants through the Las Vegas Strip.</span></p> <p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">OK, let’s run with it. </span></p> <h3><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">Gemini Enterprise Agent Platform: A warm up</span></h3> <p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">As the evolution of Vertex AI, </span><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Agent Platform</strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> “allows you to build autonomous agents that proactively help users — and complete tasks independently,” said Brad Calder, President, GCP and SRE. The platform does so with a whole suite of tools and capabilities to build, scale, govern, and optimize your agents. </span></p></div> <div class="block-image_full_width"> <div class="article-module h-c-page"> <div class="h-c-grid"> <figure class="article-image--large h-c-grid__col h-c-grid__col--6 h-c-grid__col--offset-3 " > <img src="https://storage.googleapis.com/gweb-cloudblog-publish/images/1_cBnVOvk.max-1000x1000.jpg" alt="1"> </a> </figure> </div> </div> </div> <div class="block-paragraph_advanced"><p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">Brad then passed the baton to keynote emcees Richard Seroter, Chief Evangelist, and Emma Twersky, Developer Relations Engineer, for an in-depth run-through of the agentic marathon simulator.</span></p> <p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">The system uses three main agents: A planner to determine routes; an evaluator that assesses routes based on business and community requirements; and a simulator that takes the route, adding actors and randomized behaviors to test the impact on the city,</span></p> <p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">This, Emma said, turns out to be “a great example of how agents can help us plan, simulate, and think about solving a really big challenge.” </span></p></div> <div class="block-image_full_width"> <div class="article-module h-c-page"> <div class="h-c-grid"> <figure class="article-image--large h-c-grid__col h-c-grid__col--6 h-c-grid__col--offset-3 " > <img src="https://storage.googleapis.com/gweb-cloudblog-publish/images/2_u7NylGU.max-1000x1000.jpg" alt="2"> </a> </figure> </div> </div> </div> <div class="block-paragraph_advanced"><h3><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">First off the blocks: Building the agent</span></h3> <p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">Mofi Rahman, Developer Relations Engineer, came onstage to demo how the </span><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Agent Development Kit (ADK)</strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">, Google Cloud remote </span><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Model Context Protocol (MCP) servers</strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">, and </span><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Agent Runtime</strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> provide the planner agent with the </span><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Instructions</strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">, </span><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Skills</strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">, and </span><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Tools</strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> it needs to improve the initial agent. By the end of the demo, the simulator had generated a route. </span></p> <p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">“The simulated route looks beautiful,” said Mofi. “Looks like the runners are going to get an amazing view of the entire Las Vegas Strip.”</span></p></div> <div class="block-image_full_width"> <div class="article-module h-c-page"> <div class="h-c-grid"> <figure class="article-image--large h-c-grid__col h-c-grid__col--6 h-c-grid__col--offset-3 " > <img src="https://storage.googleapis.com/gweb-cloudblog-publish/images/3_Fz2OBHO.max-1000x1000.jpg" alt="3"> </a> </figure> </div> </div> </div> <div class="block-paragraph_advanced"><h3><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">An agent to evaluate the agent</span></h3> <p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">Next, Ivan Nardini, Developer Relations Engineer, and Casey West, Architecture Advocate, showed us how to evaluate the agent, and build a UI for it. “We want to show you how to move from fragile, unpredictable agentic loops, to a rigorously evaluated network of experts that literally build their own UI,” Casey said.</span></p> <p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">They did so by deploying a separate model to judge the route, checking both deterministic (e.g., route length) and non-deterministic (e.g., community impact) criteria. For UI development, they showed off the </span><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Agent-to-User Interface</strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">, or </span><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">A2UI</strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">, an open-source standard developed by Google that created an interface in a single shot. They also used the </span><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Agent-to-Agent Protocol</strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">, or </span><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">A2A</strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">, and Agent Platform’s </span><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Agent Registry</strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">, to connect and see which agents are deployed. </span></p> <p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">“Think of Agent Registry as the DNS of your internet of agents,” Casey said. </span></p> <h3><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">Agents that never forget</span></h3> <p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">Richard then mused about how to build agents that get better with time, that “take the learnings from the simulation and optimize for the next run.” Because the answer shouldn’t be to “cram raw text in every request we send back to our agents.” </span></p> <p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">To capture this learned knowledge, Agent Platform offers </span><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Agent Platform Sessions</strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> and </span><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Memory Bank</strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">, plus the ability to turn to tools like Spark or a database to retrieve more information, resulting in an even stronger simulator.</span></p></div> <div class="block-paragraph_advanced"><h3><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">When agents go off course</span></h3> <p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">Thus far, everything had gone swimmingly, but then Richard accidentally “broke” the simulator agent. That provided a perfect opportunity for Megan O’Keefe, Senior Staff Developer Advocate, to show off </span><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Agent Interoperability</strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> and </span><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Gemini Cloud Assist</strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">, and how to use them to debug agents at scale. </span></p> <p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">“With these autonomous agents, the production challenge isn’t just scaling the infrastructure, it’s managing the reasoning, the tool calls — all the places in the system where something can go wrong!” Megan said. </span></p> <p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">Megan used </span><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Agent Runtime trace view</strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> to see where the problem was, and using natural language, launched a </span><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Cloud Assist Investigation</strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> to explore logs and events, which pointed to a specific line of code as the offender. Megan then opened up her </span><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Antigravity IDE</strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> (powered by </span><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Gemini 3</strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">, and connected via MCP) to find the problem (an insufficiently run “event compaction” run) and to suggest a fix (add a token_threshold parameter to the event compaction config). She approved the fix and committed it to source, triggering a redeployment to </span><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Agent Platform</strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">. Problem solved!</span></p> <h3><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">Scaling the agents</span></h3> <p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">To this point, all of the presenters had been showing off agent services running as </span><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Cloud Run</strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> services. Bobby Allen, Group Product Manager, then showed how to convert the apps to </span><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Google Kubernetes Engine (GKE)</strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">, which provides greater control, as well as to use a customized </span><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Gemma 4</strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> model, all by vibe coding in the Antigravity editor, which is connected to Cloud Assist. Along the way, Bobby also migrated the agents from </span><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">GCSFuse</strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> to a high-performance </span><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Lustre </strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">file system. </span></p> <p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">Closely related to scaling is sharing — making agents available for the world to use and build on. Ines Envid, Senior Director, Product Management and Jason Davenport, Area Technical Lead, showed how to build no-code agents from the </span><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Gemini Enterprise</strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> app, and how to integrate them with other, “high-code” agents. </span></p> <h3><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">Shifting down</span></h3> <p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">Last but not least, it was time to talk about security and governance. “Agents give users and other agents new ways to intentionally — or unintentionally — expose data and behavior in ways that we may not want,” mused Emma. </span></p> <p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">The standard response to that is to “shift left” — move testing, quality, and performance evaluation earlier in the development process — but for developers, that usually means more work, Richard said. “It’s not sustainable for developers to be responsible for all the layers of the stack,” he said. Instead, “we need to shift down.”</span></p> <p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">To help, there’s </span><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Agent Identity</strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> and </span><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Agent Gateway</strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">, demoed by Ankur Kotwal, head of Cloud Developer Relations. Ankur showed how Agent Gateway uses IAM policies to ensure agent actions are only accessible by approved sources, and how Agent Identity provides each agent with a unique and immutable credential. Then, </span><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Agent Policies</strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> can be configured to provide guardrails for the agents.</span></p> <p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">Yinon Costica, Co-Founder and VP of Product at Wiz, then went a step further and showed how Wiz can scan your agent code and infrastructure, and </span><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Wiz Green Agent</strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> can suggest root cause remediations. </span></p> <p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">“It’s a full architecture for security to easily understand what you built without you having to actually explain it,” Yinon said. Better yet, he also showed using this functionality from </span><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Anthropic’s Claude Code with Opus. </strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">“With Wiz, we want to enable your choice of tools and models to fix and prevent real risks,” he said.</span></p></div> <div class="block-video"> <div class="article-module article-video "> <figure> <a class="h-c-video h-c-video--marquee" href="https://youtube.com/watch?v=A01DQ8_xy7Q" data-glue-modal-trigger="uni-modal-A01DQ8_xy7Q-" data-glue-modal-disabled-on-mobile="true"> <div class="article-video__aspect-image" style="background-image: url(https://storage.googleapis.com/gweb-cloudblog-publish/images/maxresdefault_Mz6wY0B.max-1000x1000.jpg);"> <span class="h-u-visually-hidden">Google Cloud Next &#x27;26 Developer Keynote</span> </div> <svg role="img" class="h-c-video__play h-c-icon h-c-icon--color-white"> <use xlink:href="#mi-youtube-icon"></use> </svg> </a> </figure> </div> <div class="h-c-modal--video" data-glue-modal="uni-modal-A01DQ8_xy7Q-" data-glue-modal-close-label="Close Dialog"> <a class="glue-yt-video" data-glue-yt-video-autoplay="true" data-glue-yt-video-height="99%" data-glue-yt-video-vid="A01DQ8_xy7Q" data-glue-yt-video-width="100%" href="https://youtube.com/watch?v=A01DQ8_xy7Q" ng-cloak> </a> </div> </div> <div class="block-paragraph_advanced"><h3><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">The finish line</span></h3> <p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">With this, the developer keynote came to an end. But for Google Cloud developers, it’s just the beginning, as the entire solution is available as source code in GitHub, and all the </span><a href="https://codelabs.developers.google.com/next26/dev-keynote/build-multi-agent-marathon-planner#0" rel="noopener" target="_blank"><span style="text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">demos are available as Codelabs</span></a><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">. Because when it comes to agentic development, these resources will really help you hit the ground running. </span></p></div>Thu, 23 Apr 2026 13:00:00 +0000https://cloud.google.com/blog/topics/google-cloud-next/next26-day-2-recap/AI & Machine LearningApplication DevelopmentGoogle Cloud NextarticleDay 2 at Google Cloud Next: A marathon developer keynotehttps://storage.googleapis.com/gweb-cloudblog-publish/images/GCNEXT2026_0423_102940-5172_ALIVE.max-600x600.jpgGooglehttps://cloud.google.com/blog/topics/google-cloud-next/next26-day-2-recap/Google Cloud Content & Editorial Day 1 at Google Cloud Next ‘26 recaphttps://cloud.google.com/blog/topics/google-cloud-next/next26-day-1-recap/<div class="block-paragraph_advanced"><p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">Last year at Google Cloud Next ‘25, we asked you to imagine a new future for AI. At Next ‘26, the question before you is how do you move AI into production across your entire enterprise?</span></p> <p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">According to Google Cloud CEO Thomas Kurian, the answer is straightforward: You need a unified stack, with “chips that are designed for models, models that are grounded in your data, agents and applications that are built with those models,” and the whole thing “secured by the infrastructure,” Thomas said in his keynote. (This is the same unified stack that Google uses for Search, YouTube, Chrome, and Android. As Alphabet CEO Sundar Pichai said in his opening remarks, “a big focus of ours  is to always be customer zero for our own technologies.”)</span></p> <p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">As AI matures, we’ve laid out a blueprint on how to succeed. Read on for a whirlwind tour of what we announced from the keynote stage</span><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">.</span></p></div> <div class="block-video"> <div class="article-module article-video "> <figure> <a class="h-c-video h-c-video--marquee" href="https://youtube.com/watch?v=11PBno-cJ1g" data-glue-modal-trigger="uni-modal-11PBno-cJ1g-" data-glue-modal-disabled-on-mobile="true"> <div class="article-video__aspect-image" style="background-image: url(https://storage.googleapis.com/gweb-cloudblog-publish/images/next26_live_stream.max-1000x1000.jpg);"> <span class="h-u-visually-hidden">Google Cloud Next &#x27;26 Opening Keynote</span> </div> <svg role="img" class="h-c-video__play h-c-icon h-c-icon--color-white"> <use xlink:href="#mi-youtube-icon"></use> </svg> </a> </figure> </div> <div class="h-c-modal--video" data-glue-modal="uni-modal-11PBno-cJ1g-" data-glue-modal-close-label="Close Dialog"> <a class="glue-yt-video" data-glue-yt-video-autoplay="true" data-glue-yt-video-height="99%" data-glue-yt-video-vid="11PBno-cJ1g" data-glue-yt-video-width="100%" href="https://youtube.com/watch?v=11PBno-cJ1g" ng-cloak> </a> </div> </div> <div class="block-paragraph_advanced"><h3><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">Gemini Enterprise: The end-to-end system for the agentic era</span></h3> <p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">Throughout this unified stack is Gemini Enterprise — “the connective tissue between your data, your people, and your goals,” Thomas said, providing a combination of intelligence and automation across multiple layers. Here’s what’s new.</span></p></div> <div class="block-image_full_width"> <div class="article-module h-c-page"> <div class="h-c-grid"> <figure class="article-image--large h-c-grid__col h-c-grid__col--6 h-c-grid__col--offset-3 " > <img src="https://storage.googleapis.com/gweb-cloudblog-publish/images/GCNEXT2026_0422_103840-5416_ALIVE.max-1000x1000.jpg" alt="GCNEXT2026_0422_103840-5416_ALIVE"> </a> </figure> </div> </div> </div> <div class="block-paragraph_advanced"><h3 role="presentation"><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">1. Gemini Enterprise Agent Platform</span></h3> <p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">Gemini Enterprise Agent Platform is where you go to build, scale, govern, and optimize agents. As the evolution of Vertex AI, it’s built on top of our leading infrastructure, and deeply integrated with our data and security capabilities — the foundation of the Agentic Enterprise. Here’s a sampling of Agent Platform’s new features and capabilities:</span></p> <ul> <li aria-level="1" style="list-style-type: disc; vertical-align: baseline;"> <p role="presentation"><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Build:</strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> Choose the right environment for the job — from the low-code, visual interface of the new </span><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Agent Studio</strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">, to the code-first logic of the upgraded </span><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Agent Development Kit (ADK)</strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">. We’ve simplified the entire lifecycle with AI-native coding capabilities to help you ship production-grade agents faster.</span></p> </li> <li aria-level="1" style="list-style-type: disc; vertical-align: baseline;"> <p role="presentation"><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Scale:</strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> Clear the path to production with the re-engineered </span><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Agent Runtime</strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">. This supports long-running agents that maintain state for days at a time and are backed by </span><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Memory Bank</strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> for persistent, long-term context.</span></p> </li> <li aria-level="1" style="list-style-type: disc; vertical-align: baseline;"> <p role="presentation"><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Govern:</strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> Establish centralized control with </span><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Agent Identity</strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">, </span><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Agent Registry</strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">, and </span><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Agent Gateway</strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">. These capabilities help ensure every agent — whether built on Agent Platform or sourced from our partner ecosystem — has a trackable identity and operates within enterprise-grade guardrails. </span></p> </li> <li aria-level="1" style="list-style-type: disc; vertical-align: baseline;"> <p role="presentation"><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Optimize:</strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> Guarantee quality with </span><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Agent Simulation</strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">, </span><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Agent Evaluation</strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">, and </span><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Agent Observability</strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">. These tools provide full execution traces and a real-time lens into agent reasoning to help ensure your agents always hit their goals.</span></p> </li> </ul> <p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">To dive deep into Agent Platform, read more in our announcement blog </span><a href="https://cloud.google.com/blog/products/ai-machine-learning/introducing-gemini-enterprise-agent-platform"><span style="text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">here</span></a><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">. </span></p> <h3 role="presentation"><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">2. Gemini Enterprise app</span></h3></div> <div class="block-image_full_width"> <div class="article-module h-c-page"> <div class="h-c-grid"> <figure class="article-image--large h-c-grid__col h-c-grid__col--6 h-c-grid__col--offset-3 " > <img src="https://storage.googleapis.com/gweb-cloudblog-publish/images/GCNEXT2026_0422_091032-8701_ALIVE.max-1000x1000.jpg" alt="GCNEXT2026_0422_091032-8701_ALIVE"> </a> </figure> </div> </div> </div> <div class="block-paragraph_advanced"><p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">The Gemini Enterprise app is</span><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> “the primary environment where your business actually operates,” Thomas explained. The app is where many workers, especially non-technical ones, can ask questions of enterprise agents, create generative media, engage with prebuilt agents, and even create their own with conversational interfaces — all with governance, compliance, and security built in. </span><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">Here’s a sample of what’s new in this foundational interface: </span></p> <ul> <li aria-level="1" style="list-style-type: disc; vertical-align: baseline;"> <p role="presentation"><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Gemini Enterprise Projects </strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">give your agents permanent memory.</span></p> </li> <li aria-level="1" style="list-style-type: disc; vertical-align: baseline;"> <p role="presentation"><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Deep Think </strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">solves your most complex business challenges without context pollution.</span></p> </li> <li aria-level="1" style="list-style-type: disc; vertical-align: baseline;"> <p role="presentation"><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Microsoft 365 </strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">interoperability makes it easy to export docs you create with Canvas into Microsoft Office formats.</span></p> </li> </ul> <p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">To illustrate the power of Gemini Enterprise, Shaun White, three-time Olympic gold medalist, entrepreneur, and snowboarding legend, joined us on stage.</span></p> <p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">“Back when I was training, our tools were camcorders and guesswork. You’d land a trick and watch it back. And you’d be thinking, ‘How can I make that trick better?’” he said.  </span></p> <p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">Alongside Jason Davenport, Google Cloud Tech Lead, they showed a model that Google Cloud built in collaboration with Google DeepMind that tracked Shaun in space from a two-dimensional video, helping him understand what he was doing right and wrong. </span></p> <p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">“Learning the trick on the mountain is one thing, but actually understanding the physics of a trick is a whole other thing,” Shaun said.  </span></p> <p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">Read more on the Gemini Enterprise app </span><a href="https://cloud.google.com/blog/products/ai-machine-learning/whats-new-in-gemini-enterprise?e=48754805"><span style="text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">here</span></a><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">. </span></p></div> <div class="block-image_full_width"> <div class="article-module h-c-page"> <div class="h-c-grid"> <figure class="article-image--large h-c-grid__col h-c-grid__col--6 h-c-grid__col--offset-3 " > <img src="https://storage.googleapis.com/gweb-cloudblog-publish/images/GCNEXT2026_0422_093546-4510_ALIVE.max-1000x1000.jpg" alt="Shaun White"> </a> </figure> </div> </div> </div> <div class="block-paragraph_advanced"><div data-draftjs-conductor-fragment='{"blocks":[{"key":"dsr0p","text":"3. AI Hypercomputer","type":"unstyled","depth":0,"inlineStyleRanges":[],"entityRanges":[],"data":{}},{"key":"4v39t","text":"The same technology foundation that athletes like Shaun White use to understand their performance is being used by enterprises to transform their businesses. ","type":"unstyled","depth":0,"inlineStyleRanges":[],"entityRanges":[],"data":{}},{"key":"fhjv0","text":"Amin Vadhat, SVP and chief technologist, AI and Infrastructure, took to the stage to announce enhancements to AI Hypercomputer, the integrated supercomputing underneath every AI workload on Google Cloud.","type":"unstyled","depth":0,"inlineStyleRanges":[],"entityRanges":[{"offset":110,"length":16,"key":0}],"data":{}}],"entityMap":{"0":{"type":"LINK","mutability":"MUTABLE","data":{"url":"https://cloud.google.com/solutions/ai-hypercomputer"}}}}'> <div class="Draftail-block--unstyled" data-block="true" data-editor="fujua" data-offset-key="ma2lh-0-0"> <h3 class="public-DraftStyleDefault-block public-DraftStyleDefault-ltr" data-offset-key="ma2lh-0-0"><span data-offset-key="ma2lh-0-0">3. AI Hypercomputer</span></h3> </div> <div class="Draftail-block--unstyled" data-block="true" data-editor="fujua" data-offset-key="25o56-0-0"> <div class="public-DraftStyleDefault-block public-DraftStyleDefault-ltr" data-offset-key="25o56-0-0"><span data-offset-key="25o56-0-0">The same technology foundation that athletes like Shaun White use to understand their performance is being used by enterprises to transform their businesses. </span></div> </div> <div class="Draftail-block--unstyled" data-block="true" data-editor="fujua" data-offset-key="et8mb-0-0"> <div class="public-DraftStyleDefault-block public-DraftStyleDefault-ltr" data-offset-key="et8mb-0-0"> </div> <div class="public-DraftStyleDefault-block public-DraftStyleDefault-ltr" data-offset-key="et8mb-0-0"><span data-offset-key="et8mb-0-0">Amin Vadhat, SVP and chief technologist, AI and Infrastructure, took to the stage to announce enhancements to </span><a class="TooltipEntity" data-draftail-trigger="true" href="https://cloud.google.com/solutions/ai-hypercomputer" role="button"><span data-offset-key="et8mb-1-0">AI Hypercomputer</span></a><span data-offset-key="et8mb-2-0">, the integrated supercomputing underneath every AI workload on Google Cloud.</span></div> </div> </div></div> <div class="block-image_full_width"> <div class="article-module h-c-page"> <div class="h-c-grid"> <figure class="article-image--large h-c-grid__col h-c-grid__col--6 h-c-grid__col--offset-3 " > <img src="https://storage.googleapis.com/gweb-cloudblog-publish/images/GCNEXT2026_0422_094223-0331_ALIVE.max-1000x1000.jpg" alt="GCNEXT2026_0422_094223-0331_ALIVE"> </a> </figure> </div> </div> </div> <div class="block-paragraph_advanced"><p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">First, there’s the eighth-generation Tensor Processing Unit, or TPU — “a thing of beauty,” Amin said. And because “the demands of training and serving have completely diverged,” this TPU family actually consists of two chips: </span></p> <ul> <li aria-level="1" style="list-style-type: disc; vertical-align: baseline;"> <p role="presentation"><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">TPU 8t, optimized for training</strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">, uses new Inter-Chip Interconnect (ICI) technology to scale up to 9,600 TPUs and 2 petabytes of shared, high-bandwidth memory in a single superpod. It achieves three times the processing power of Ironwood and delivers up to double the performance per watt. </span></p> </li> <li aria-level="1" style="list-style-type: disc; vertical-align: baseline;"> <p role="presentation"><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">TPU 8i, optimized for inference</strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">, uses the new Boardfly topology to directly connect 1,152 TPUs in a single pod. It features three times more on-chip SRAM compared to previous versions and a specialized Collectives Acceleration Engine offloads resource-heavy tasks. Taken together, TPU 8i delivers 80% better performance per dollar for inference than the prior generation, helping </span><a href="https://cloud.google.com/blog/products/compute/tpu-8t-and-tpu-8i-technical-deep-dive"><span style="text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">millions of concurrent agents to run cost-effectively</span></a><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">.</span></p> </li> </ul> <p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">AI Hypercomputer also supports Arm-based Google Cloud Axion processors, such as the </span><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">N4A, now generally available</strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">, and will be one of the first platforms to offer </span><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">NVIDIA’s Vera Rubin NVL72</strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> platform when it is released.</span></p> <p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">Other parts of the network need to keep up with the demands of the agentic era. For example, the new </span><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Virgo Network</strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> doubles connectivity to scale training beyond AI Hypercomputer superpods, and </span><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Google Cloud Managed Lustre</strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> now supports an industry-leading 10 terabytes per second of throughput. </span></p> <p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">Learn more about all of our AI infrastructure innovations </span><a href="https://cloud.google.com/blog/products/compute/ai-infrastructure-at-next26?e=48754805"><span style="text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">here</span></a><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">. </span></p> <h3 role="presentation"><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">4. Agentic Data Cloud</span></h3> <p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">The AI era hinges on data. Lots of data. That data comes with a catch: It needs to be grounded in context. That’s because “reasoning without context is just a guess,” explained Karthik Narain, chief product and business officer.</span></p></div> <div class="block-image_full_width"> <div class="article-module h-c-page"> <div class="h-c-grid"> <figure class="article-image--large h-c-grid__col h-c-grid__col--6 h-c-grid__col--offset-3 " > <img src="https://storage.googleapis.com/gweb-cloudblog-publish/images/GCNEXT2026_0422_085702-_ALIVE.max-1000x1000.jpg" alt="GCNEXT2026_0422_085702-_ALIVE"> </a> </figure> </div> </div> </div> <div class="block-paragraph_advanced"><p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">To that end, we’re totally rethinking our data platform, and giving it a new name: the Agentic Data Cloud.</span></p> <p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">Here’s a sampling of what you’ll find in the Agentic Data Cloud:</span></p> <ul> <li aria-level="1" style="list-style-type: disc; vertical-align: baseline;"> <p role="presentation"><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Knowledge Catalog</strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> constructs a unified, dynamic context graph of your entire business enabling you to ground agents in all of your business data and semantics. With </span><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Smart Storage</strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> and the Object Context API, files in Google Cloud Storage are instantly tagged and enriched with metadata before an agent touches them. Knowledge Catalog is also integrated with Gemini’s </span><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Deep Research Agent</strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">.</span></p> </li> <li aria-level="1" style="list-style-type: disc; vertical-align: baseline;"> <p role="presentation"><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Data Agent Kit</strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> delivers a Gemini-powered data science authoring experience across your IDEs, Notebooks, and agentic terminals. </span></p> </li> <li aria-level="1" style="list-style-type: disc; vertical-align: baseline;"> <p role="presentation"><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Lightning Engine for Apache Spark </strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">is a real-time, serverless engine that is up to 4.5 times faster than open-source alternatives and offers up to double price-performance over the leading competitor for large datasets.</span></p> </li> <li aria-level="1" style="list-style-type: disc; vertical-align: baseline;"> <p role="presentation"><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">Finally, </span><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Cross-Cloud Lakehouse</strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">, based on Apache Iceberg, lets you query data in Amazon Web Services or Azure without having to copy it.</span></p> </li> </ul> <p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">Learn all about all the innovations in the Agentic Data Cloud </span><a href="https://cloud.google.com/blog/products/data-analytics/whats-new-in-the-agentic-data-cloud?e=48754805"><span style="text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">here</span></a><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">. </span></p> <h3><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">5. Agentic Defense</span></h3> <p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">AI makes — and demands — that everything go faster, and security operations are no exception. Increasingly, “human analysts can’t keep up with AI-driven attacks,” said Francis deSouza, COO, and president, Security Products. </span></p> <p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">“Security must become an autonomous force, responding faster than the threat itself,” he said. </span></p> <p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">To help, we introduced three new agents in </span><a href="https://cloud.google.com/security/products/security-operations"><span style="text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">Google Security Operations</span></a><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> to help you defend at the speed of AI. </span></p> <ul> <li aria-level="1" style="list-style-type: disc; vertical-align: baseline;"> <p role="presentation"><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Threat Hunting agent</strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">: Helps teams proactively hunt for novel attack patterns and stealthy adversary behaviors that bypass traditional defenses. Now in preview. </span></p> </li> <li aria-level="1" style="list-style-type: disc; vertical-align: baseline;"> <p role="presentation"><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Detection Engineering agent</strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">: Identifies coverage gaps and creates new detections for threat scenarios. Now in preview. </span></p> </li> <li aria-level="1" style="list-style-type: disc; vertical-align: baseline;"> <p role="presentation"><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Third-Party Context agent: </strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">Enriches workflows with contextual data from third-party content. Coming soon to preview.</span></p> </li> </ul> <p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">You can also </span><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">build your own security agents</strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> with remote Google Cloud MCP server support for Google Security Operations, now generally available, and access it from the Google Security Operations chat interface, now in preview.</span></p></div> <div class="block-image_full_width"> <div class="article-module h-c-page"> <div class="h-c-grid"> <figure class="article-image--large h-c-grid__col h-c-grid__col--6 h-c-grid__col--offset-3 " > <img src="https://storage.googleapis.com/gweb-cloudblog-publish/images/GCNEXT2026_0422_100749-9822_ALIVE.max-1000x1000.jpg" alt="GCNEXT2026_0422_100749-9822_ALIVE"> </a> </figure> </div> </div> </div> <div class="block-paragraph_advanced"><p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">Then there’s </span><a href="https://cloud.google.com/blog/products/identity-security/google-completes-acquisition-of-wiz?e=48754805"><span style="text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">Wiz, now a part of Google Cloud</span></a><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">, whose AI-Application Protection Platform (AI-APP), Wiz Security Agents, and Wiz Workflow help you identify and respond to risks and threats at machine speed. New in the Wiz family today are</span><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">:  </span></p> <ul> <li aria-level="1" style="list-style-type: disc; vertical-align: baseline;"> <p role="presentation"><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Secure vibe-coded applications: </strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">A new integration runs Wiz security scanning directly inside the Lovable platform so vulnerabilities, secrets, and misconfigurations caught by Wiz surface in Lovable's built-in security view. Generally available in May.</span></p> </li> <li aria-level="1" style="list-style-type: disc; vertical-align: baseline;"> <p role="presentation"><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Secure AI-generated code</strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">: Wiz can now remove risks from AI-generated code with inline AI security hooks integrated directly into IDEs and agent workflows, injecting security guardrails before code is committed.</span></p> </li> <li aria-level="1" style="list-style-type: disc; vertical-align: baseline;"> <p role="presentation"><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Agent-based remediation</strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">: Wiz Skills can equip coding agents and AI-native IDEs with full code-to-cloud context and validated attack surface findings from the Wiz Security Graph.</span></p> </li> <li aria-level="1" style="list-style-type: disc; vertical-align: baseline;"> <p role="presentation"><a href="https://www.wiz.io/academy/ai-security/ai-bom-ai-bill-of-materials" rel="noopener" target="_blank"><strong style="text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">AI-Bill of Materials</strong></a><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;"> (AI-BOM):</strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> Work towards eliminating shadow IT by automatically inventorying all AI frameworks, models, and IDE extensions across your environment.</span></p> </li> <li aria-level="1" style="list-style-type: disc; vertical-align: baseline;"> <p role="presentation"><a href="https://cloud.google.com/blog/products/identity-security/introducing-google-cloud-fraud-defense-the-next-evolution-of-recaptcha"><strong style="text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">Google Cloud Fraud Defense</strong></a><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">: The evolution of reCAPTCHA, this platform is designed to discern the legitimacy and authorization of bots, humans, and agents. Now generally available.</span></p> </li> </ul> <p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">Read more about these security innovations </span><a href="https://cloud.google.com/blog/products/identity-security/next26-redefining-security-for-the-ai-era-with-google-cloud-and-wiz?e=48754805"><span style="text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">here</span></a><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">. </span></p> <h3 role="presentation"><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">6. Workspace Intelligence</span></h3> <p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">For a look at AI for end-users, we heard from Yulie Kwon Kim, VP, Product, Google Workspace, who shared new ways that AI is manifesting in our collaboration and productivity suite. </span><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Workspace Intelligence </strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">is a unifying semantic layer that breaks down information and context silos for you and your agents. It understands your work, your priorities and the people you work with to help you get more done. </span></p></div> <div class="block-image_full_width"> <div class="article-module h-c-page"> <div class="h-c-grid"> <figure class="article-image--large h-c-grid__col h-c-grid__col--6 h-c-grid__col--offset-3 " > <img src="https://storage.googleapis.com/gweb-cloudblog-publish/images/GCNEXT2026_0422_102731-1098_ALIVE.max-1000x1000.jpg" alt="GCNEXT2026_0422_102731-1098_ALIVE"> </a> </figure> </div> </div> </div> <div class="block-paragraph_advanced"><p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">“Think of it as a unified intelligence layer that lives inside every Workspace app. It connects the dots and lets AI do the heavy lifting," Yulie said.</span></p> <p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">Here’s what’s new:</span></p> <p><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Ask Gemini in Google Chat </strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">allows you to instantly synthesize information, surface insights, and query projects from across Workspace directly from your Google Chat window. It provides proactive daily briefings to help you prioritize, and also lets you take immediate action — such as scheduling a meeting on your calendar or creating a Google Doc to develop a pre-meeting brief — turning your conversations into momentum without having to switch tabs.</span></p></div> <div class="block-video"> <div class="article-module article-video "> <figure> <a class="h-c-video h-c-video--marquee" href="https://youtube.com/watch?v=YppfLqH7Fps" data-glue-modal-trigger="uni-modal-YppfLqH7Fps-" data-glue-modal-disabled-on-mobile="true"> <div class="article-video__aspect-image" style="background-image: url(https://storage.googleapis.com/gweb-cloudblog-publish/images/maxresdefault_JTY9905.max-1000x1000.jpg);"> <span class="h-u-visually-hidden">Ask Gemini in Chat</span> </div> <svg role="img" class="h-c-video__play h-c-icon h-c-icon--color-white"> <use xlink:href="#mi-youtube-icon"></use> </svg> </a> </figure> </div> <div class="h-c-modal--video" data-glue-modal="uni-modal-YppfLqH7Fps-" data-glue-modal-close-label="Close Dialog"> <a class="glue-yt-video" data-glue-yt-video-autoplay="true" data-glue-yt-video-height="99%" data-glue-yt-video-vid="YppfLqH7Fps" data-glue-yt-video-width="100%" href="https://youtube.com/watch?v=YppfLqH7Fps" ng-cloak> </a> </div> </div> <div class="block-paragraph_advanced"><ul> <li aria-level="1" style="list-style-type: disc; In addition to newly added </span><a href="https://blog.google/products-and-platforms/products/workspace/gemini-workspace-updates-march-2026/" rel="noopener" target="_blank"><span style="text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">AI Overviews and Ask Gemini</span></a><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">, Projects is another way we’re transforming Drive from a storage tool into an active collaborator to provide insights about your data.</span></p> </li> <li aria-level="1" style="list-style-type: disc; vertical-align: baseline;"> <p role="presentation"><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Workspace agent</strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> in Gemini Enterprise executes complex, multi-step tasks across Google Workspace apps without having to leave Gemini Enterprise. </span></p> </li> </ul> <p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">For more, check out the full Workspace Intelligence </span><a href="https://workspace.google.com/blog/product-announcements/introducing-workspace-intelligence?_gl=1*1lcx1ks*_up*MQ..&amp;gclid=CjwKCAjw46HPBhAMEiwASZpLRCh04El-PH-mQX3OW7IcONinrI6ZdqmWKi_j1tyhxEOFnZTaaMBr2xoCFb8QAvD_BwE&amp;gclsrc=aw.ds" rel="noopener" target="_blank"><span style="text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">blog</span></a><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">.</span></p> <h3 role="presentation"><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">7. Agentic Commerce</span></h3> <p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">For enterprises, AI agents are reshaping how consumers engage with companies and their products. </span></p> <p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">“In the agentic era, an agent isn’t just a tool; it’s a strategic extension of your business, built to expand your reach, deepen engagement, and personalize service at scale,” said Carrie Tharp, Google Cloud Vice President of Go To Market Strategic Industries. </span></p> <p><a href="https://cloud.google.com/products/gemini-enterprise-for-customer-experience"><span style="text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">Gemini Enterprise for Customer Experience</span></a><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> offers a suite of tools to enhance the entire customer journey, from the first moment of discovery through on-going interactions that remember the customer like the best shopkeeper would. </span></p> <ul> <li role="presentation"><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Shopping agent </strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">and </span><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Food Ordering agent </strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">bring new conversational sales and ordering capabilities direct to businesses and third-party chat and digital interfaces.</span></li> <li role="presentation"><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Omnichannel Gateway</strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> helps agents maintain context across web, mobile, and voice, so a company’s agents can offer more personalized service.</span></li> <li role="presentation"><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Agent Assist</strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> helps during complex customer service situations, coaching employees to deliver fast and more accurate answers to customer questions by having organizational data readily available through gen AI grounding.</span></li> </ul> <p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">With Omnichannel Gateway in particular, about bridging the physical, digital, and agentic shopping experience, so consumers always have a familiar, brand-aware experience. </span></p> <p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">“If a customer moves from text chat to a phone call, the agent seamlessly remembers exactly where they left off,” said Carrie. Now that’s progress!</span></p> <p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">For more customer stories, check out all </span><a href="https://cloud.google.com/transform/101-real-world-generative-ai-use-cases-from-industry-leaders?e=48754805"><span style="text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">1,302 of the latest gen AI use cases</span></a><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> from businesses around the globe.</span></p> <h3><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">Innovate all the things </span></h3> <p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">From new products, to new solutions, to new ways of working, there are so many other ways that we’re helping organizations take their AI from pilot to production. </span></p> <p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">Over the following week, we’ll share even more news, helpful how-to guides, and go deeper on today’s announcements. By delivering real-time, contextual intelligence through conversation, it reduces handling time, improves first-contact resolution, and enables consistent, data-driven responses.</span></p> <p style="padding-left: 40px;"><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Teradata:</strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> </span><a href="https://console.cloud.google.com/marketplace/product/teradata-public/dataanalystagent-as-a-service-v1"><span style="text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">Data Analyst AI Agent</span></a><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> enables natural-language analytics on enterprise data in Google Cloud. It translates business questions into governed SQL and Python workflows on Teradata, delivering faster, secure insights without requiring data movement.</span></p> <p style="padding-left: 40px;"><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Typeface: </strong><a href="http://console.cloud.google.com/marketplace/product/typeface-public/typeface-agent"><span style="text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">Typeface Agent</span></a><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> acts as a seamless bridge to creative campaigns. It enables instant access to Typeface teams, brand assets, and campaigns via natural language from Gemini Enterprise. Users can trigger high-quality, brand-aligned content creation workflows, streamlining the journey from ideation to production.</span></p> <p style="padding-left: 40px;"><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">UKG:</strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> </span><a href="https://console.cloud.google.com/marketplace/product/ukg-public/ukgpeopleassistagent"><span style="text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">Agentic People Assist — HR Service Delivery</span></a><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> elevates the agentic capabilities of the UKG Workforce Operating Platform by empowering employees and managers with knowledge and connected agents to turn intent into action.
