In just a few months, the number of </span><a href="https://www.databricks.com/blog/enterprise-ai-agent-trends-top-use-cases-governance-evaluations-and-more" rel="noopener" target="_blank"><span style="text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">multi-agent AI workflows has surged</span></a><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> by 327%. At the same time, </span><a href="https://thenewstack.io/cncf-kubernetes-is-foundational-infrastructure-for-ai/" rel="noopener" target="_blank"><span style="text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">66%</span></a><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> of organizations rely on Kubernetes to power generative AI apps and agents.</span></p> <p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">This new era of autonomous agents operating at massive scale requires a foundational change in how we manage infrastructure — a change that is more demanding than the shift from stateless to stateful applications. </span></p> <p><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">What’s new: </strong></p> <ul> <li aria-level="1" style="list-style-type: disc; vertical-align: baseline;"> <p role="presentation"><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">GKE Agent Sandbox:</strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> Secure, highly scalable, low-latency agent infrastructure</span></p> </li> <li aria-level="1" style="list-style-type: disc; vertical-align: baseline;"> <p role="presentation"><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">GKE hypercluster:</strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">  A single, conformant GKE control plane to manage millions of accelerators across Google Cloud regions</span></p> </li> <li aria-level="1" style="list-style-type: disc; vertical-align: baseline;"> <p role="presentation"><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Improved inference performance:</strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> Foundational enhancements to GKE Inference Gateway and KV Cache management</span></p> </li> <li aria-level="1" style="list-style-type: disc; vertical-align: baseline;"> <p role="presentation"><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Reinforcement learning (RL) enhancers: </strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">Native capabilities to relieve bottlenecks that throttle accelerator utilization </span></p> </li> <li aria-level="1" style="list-style-type: disc; vertical-align: baseline;"> <p role="presentation"><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Scaling on custom metrics:</strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> Support for intent-based autoscaling on triggers besides CPU and memory</span></p> </li> </ul> <p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">Read on for details about these GKE announcements.</span></p> <h3><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">GKE Agent Sandbox: Accelerating the agentic era</span></h3> <p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">As </span><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">AI evolves from simple conversational chatbots to entire ecosystems of proactive, autonomous agents, the underlying infrastructure must adapt to handle hundreds or thousands of agents collaborating with workers to plan, evaluate, and execute complex tasks. At scale, infrastructure performance, responsiveness, and rigorous security are essential. </span></p> <p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">We are excited to announce </span><a href="https://docs.cloud.google.com/kubernetes-engine/docs/concepts/machine-learning/agent-sandbox"><strong style="text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">GKE Agent Sandbox</strong></a><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">, the industry’s most scalable and low-latency agent infrastructure. Built with gVisor kernel isolation — the same technology securing Gemini — Agent Sandbox allows you to safely execute untrusted code, tools, and entire agents without sacrificing performance. </span><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">GKE provides leading speed and efficiency for fully isolated agents with </span><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">300 sandboxes per second at sub-second latency and up to 30% better price-performance when running on Axion compared to other hyperscale clouds.</strong></p> <p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">Lovable empowers anyone to build apps and websites — with builders creating 200,000+ new projects daily.  Lovable runs these AI-generated applications in GKE Agent Sandboxes because of the fast startup, fast scaling and secure isolation. </span></p> <p style="padding-left: 40px;"><span style="font-style: italic; vertical-align: baseline;">GKE's cutting-edge sandboxing capabilities allow us to reliably scale to hundreds of secure sandboxes per second, ensuring we can seamlessly empower builders, even during massive, unpredictable demand." </span><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">- Fabian Hedin, Co-founder, Lovable </span></p> <h3><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">GKE hypercluster redefines the scalability ceiling </span></h3> <p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">As foundational AI models grow exponentially and accelerators remain in high demand, organizations resort to fracturing Kubernetes compute infrastructure into hundreds of disconnected clusters, which can create a massive operational burden. To help, we’re announcing the private GA of </span><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">GKE hypercluster</strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">, which allows a single, Kubernetes conformant GKE control plane to manage a million chips distributed across 256,000 nodes — spanning multiple Google Cloud regions. With the GKE hypercluster, widely distributed infrastructure becomes a single, unified capacity reserve that spans geographical locations.</span></p> <p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">To scale globally without compromising security, GKE hypercluster relies on Google’s Titanium Intelligence Enclave, a software-hardened security engine that delivers private AI compute. This "no-admin-access" model provides hardware-attested, pod-level isolation, so that proprietary model weights and prompts remain cryptographically sealed from platform administrators and infrastructure layers.</span></p> <h3><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">Supercharging state-of-the-art inference</span></h3> <p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">Achieving frontier inference requires months of complex performance tuning. To reduce this heavy lifting, GKE now slashes your "time to SOTA" across TPUs and GPUs to mere minutes. We do this with new capabilities:</span></p> <ul> <li aria-level="1" style="list-style-type: disc; vertical-align: baseline;"> <p role="presentation"><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">ML-driven </span><a href="https://llm-d.ai/blog/predicted-latency-based-scheduling-for-llms" rel="noopener" target="_blank"><strong style="text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">Predictive Latency Boost</strong></a><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> in GKE Inference Gateway, which can reduce time-to-first-token latency by up 70% by replacing heuristic guesswork with real-time capacity-aware routing — no manual tuning required. </span></p> </li> <li aria-level="1" style="list-style-type: disc; vertical-align: baseline;"> <p role="presentation"><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Automatic KV Cache storage tiering</strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> across RAM, Local SSD, and GCS/Lustre solves long-context memory bottlenecks. </span><a href="https://github.com/llm-d/llm-d/blob/main/guides/tiered-prefix-cache/README.md" rel="noopener" target="_blank"><span style="text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">Offloading KV Cache</span></a><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> to RAM yielded a more than 40% TTFT reduction and a 50% throughput gain for a 10K system prompt length. Offloading KV Cache to Local SSD yielded an almost 70% throughput improvement for a 50K system prompt length. Learn more about these benchmarks in the </span><a href="https://github.com/llm-d/llm-d/blob/main/guides/tiered-prefix-cache/storage/README.md#benchmarking" rel="noopener" target="_blank"><span style="text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">llm-d Offloading Prefix Cache to Shared Storage guide</span></a><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">.</span></p> </li> </ul> <p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">Built as part of a layered composable suite, these new GKE capabilities leverage llm-d, now an official </span><a href="https://cloud.google.com/blog/products/containers-kubernetes/llm-d-officially-a-cncf-sandbox-project"><span style="text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">CNCF Sandbox project</span></a><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">. To give you maximum flexibility, we’ve partnered closely with NVIDIA to seamlessly integrate Dynamo for scaling massive </span><a href="https://cloud.google.com/blog/products/compute/scaling-moe-inference-with-nvidia-dynamo-on-google-cloud-a4x?e=48754805"><span style="text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">Mixture-of-Experts (MoE) models</span></a><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">. Whichever tools you choose, GKE provides the highly-optimized, flexible infrastructure you need to safely run any frontier AI workload — including the advanced agentic capabilities of the newly announced </span><a href="https://cloud.google.com/blog/products/ai-machine-learning/gemma-4-available-on-google-cloud?e=48754805"><span style="text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">Gemma 4</span></a><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">.</span></p> <h3><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">Eliminating RL compute bottlenecks</span></h3> <p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">Reinforcement learning (RL) is a key driver of AI compute demand and RL jobs involve sequential processing for sampling, reward, and training that can leave GPU and TPU accelerators idle between these RL steps. To streamline RL, we are adding new GKE capabilities in preview:</span></p> <ul> <li aria-level="1" style="list-style-type: disc; vertical-align: baseline;"> <p role="presentation"><a href="https://github.com/llm-d-incubation/py-inference-scheduler" rel="noopener" target="_blank"><strong style="text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">RL Scheduler</strong></a><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> solves for the "straggler effect" and inter-batch tail latency, maximizing throughput via intelligent routing.  </span></p> </li> <li aria-level="1" style="list-style-type: disc; vertical-align: baseline;"> <p role="presentation"><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">RL Sandbox</strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> provides kernel-level isolation for tool-calling and reward evaluation with millisecond-scale provisioning. Easy integration with RL sampling and reward steps.</span></p> </li> <li aria-level="1" style="list-style-type: disc; vertical-align: baseline;"> <p role="presentation"><a href="https://docs.cloud.google.com/kubernetes-engine/docs/tutorials/monitor-reinforcement-learning-workloads"><strong style="text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">RL Observability and Reliability</strong></a><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> dashboards offer the deep visibility required to troubleshoot and optimize the entire RL loop instantly, out of the box.</span></p> </li> </ul> <p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">Review the RL on GKE recipe, specifically the implementations for </span><a href="https://docs.cloud.google.com/kubernetes-engine/docs/tutorials/scaling-rl-verl-gke"><span style="text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">Verl</span></a><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> and </span><a href="https://docs.cloud.google.com/kubernetes-engine/docs/tutorials/nemo-rl-gke"><span style="text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">NeMo RL</span></a><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">.</span></p> <h3><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">Intent-based autoscaling on custom metrics</span></h3> <p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">Traditionally, scaling AI workloads based on application health has imposed a "custom metric tax." To scale the system on anything but basic compute or memory utilization, organizations have to manage complex monitoring systems and IAM roles. This creates operational risk: if your external observability stack fails, your autoscaling breaks along with it.</span></p> <p><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Intent-based autoscaling</strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> eliminates this overhead via native </span><a href="https://docs.cloud.google.com/kubernetes-engine/docs/how-to/expose-custom-metrics-autoscaling"><strong style="text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">custom metrics support</strong></a><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;"> for GKE’s Horizontal Pod Autoscaler (HPA)</strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">. This agentless architecture bypasses external dependencies by sourcing metrics directly from Pods, hardening reliability while cutting costs. Crucially, it drops reaction times from 25 seconds to just 5 seconds—a </span><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">5x </span><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> performance gain for near-instantaneous infrastructure elasticity.</span></p> <h3><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">New workloads, same mission</span></h3> <p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">For over a decade, GKE has set the standard for scalable infrastructure. As we enter the era of agentic and autonomous AI, our mission remains the same: eliminating operational friction so you can focus on innovation. The capabilities we are announcing at Next ‘26 — from GKE hypercluster and the Agent Sandbox, to ultra-fast inference and intent-based autoscaling — give you the secure, efficient, and powerful engine you need to succeed with your ambitious AI workloads. To learn more about using GKE for your AI workloads, check out </span><a href="https://cloud.google.com/kubernetes-engine/docs/how-to/machine-learning/inference/inference-quickstart"><span style="text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">GKE Inference Quickstart</span></a><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">. </span></p></div>Wed, 22 Apr 2026 12:00:00 +0000https://cloud.google.com/blog/products/containers-kubernetes/whats-new-in-gke-at-next26/AI & Machine LearningApplication DevelopmentGKEGoogle Cloud NextContainers & KubernetesarticleWhat’s new in GKE at Next ‘26https://storage.googleapis.com/gweb-cloudblog-publish/images/GCN26_102_BlogHeader_2436x1200_Opt_13_Dark.max-600x600.jpgGooglehttps://cloud.google.com/blog/products/containers-kubernetes/whats-new-in-gke-at-next26/Drew BradstockSr. Director, Orchestration and Kubernetes Product ManagementGari SinghGKE Group Product ManagerIntroducing Virgo Network, Google’s scale-out AI data center fabrichttps://cloud.google.com/blog/products/networking/introducing-virgo-megascale-data-center-fabric/<div class="block-paragraph_advanced"><p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">The AI era requires a fundamental rethink of physical cloud architecture — networking, in particular. With foundational model parameters growing exponentially, traditional general-purpose networks are reaching their breaking points. To fuel the next decade of machine learning, Google designed Virgo Network, a new megascale AI data center fabric that embraces a "campus-as-a-computer" philosophy, and that underpins our </span><a href="https://cloud.google.com/solutions/ai-hypercomputer?e=48754805"><span style="text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">AI Hypercomputer</span></a><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">.</span></p> <p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">Legacy network designs simply cannot handle some of the constraints of modern AI:</span></p> <ol> <li aria-level="1" style="list-style-type: decimal; vertical-align: baseline;"> <p role="presentation"><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Massive scale:</strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> Training demands now exceed the power and space of a single data center, requiring unified, multi-data-center domains.</span></p> </li> <li aria-level="1" style="list-style-type: decimal; vertical-align: baseline;"> <p role="presentation"><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Explosive bandwidth growth:</strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> Because foundational model training is heavily network-bound, the required bandwidth per accelerator has surged significantly over the last few years, creating throughput and congestion bottlenecks for older architectures.</span></p> </li> <li aria-level="1" style="list-style-type: decimal; vertical-align: baseline;"> <p role="presentation"><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Synchronized bursts:</strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> Intense, millisecond-level traffic spikes (figure 1) put immense pressure on network buffers. The outcome is that even a single "straggler" node can throttle the entire cluster’s performance.</span></p> </li> <li><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Low latency: </strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">ML serving requires fast, consistent response times to deliver real-time inference, making strict latency control a critical architectural constraint.</span></li> </ol></div> <div class="block-image_full_width"> <div class="article-module h-c-page"> <div class="h-c-grid"> <figure class="article-image--large h-c-grid__col h-c-grid__col--6 h-c-grid__col--offset-3 " > <img src="https://storage.googleapis.com/gweb-cloudblog-publish/images/1_Sub-millisecond_line-rate_bursts_of_an_A.max-1000x1000.png" alt="1 Sub-millisecond line-rate bursts of an AI training workload"> </a> <figcaption class="article-image__caption "><p data-block-key="s0df9">Figure 1: Sub-millisecond line-rate bursts of an AI training workload</p></figcaption> </figure> </div> </div> </div> <div class="block-paragraph_advanced"><h3><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">Reimagining the data center network</span></h3> <p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">Meeting the demands of the AI era requires a fundamental shift away from general-purpose network design towards a specialized flat, low-latency network architecture. To address the unique scale and latency constraints, we leverage our proven </span><a href="https://cloud.google.com/blog/products/networking/speed-scale-reliability-25-years-of-data-center-networking?e=48754805"><span style="text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">Jupiter</span></a><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> network for north-south traffic and are introducing a new fabric for east-west communication. The resulting architecture consists of three distinct and specialized layers that operate as one unified compute domain:</span></p> <ol> <li aria-level="1" style="list-style-type: decimal; vertical-align: baseline;"> <p role="presentation"><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Scale-up domain:</strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> A high-bandwidth, low-latency interconnect fabric designed for tightly coupled communication between accelerators within a single pod. </span></p> </li> <li aria-level="1" style="list-style-type: decimal; vertical-align: baseline;"> <p role="presentation"><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Scale-out accelerator fabric (east-west):</strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> A dedicated accelerator-to-accelerator remote direct memory access (RDMA) fabric optimized for massive horizontal scale across pods. This layer is engineered for deterministic latency and maximum resilience, to provide high “</span><a href="https://cloud.google.com/blog/products/ai-machine-learning/goodput-metric-as-measure-of-ml-productivity"><span style="text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">goodput</span></a><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">” for the ML workload.</span></p> </li> <li aria-level="1" style="list-style-type: decimal; vertical-align: baseline;"> <p role="presentation"><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Jupiter front-end network (north-south):</strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> A high-capacity fabric that provides fast, reliable access to distributed storage and general-purpose compute resources. It ensures that data access does not become a bottleneck for training and serving workloads, and is also used to scale-across multiple sites for very large training runs.</span></p> </li> </ol> <p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">This architectural decoupling provides key strategic advantages:</span></p> <ol> <li aria-level="1" style="list-style-type: decimal; vertical-align: baseline;"> <p role="presentation"><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Independent evolution:</strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> We can evolve and upgrade each network domain independently, preventing system-wide disruptions while accelerating the innovation cycle. </span></p> </li> <li aria-level="1" style="list-style-type: decimal; vertical-align: baseline;"> <p role="presentation"><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Dedicated scale-out bandwidth:</strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> A non-blocking network delivers massive bisectional bandwidth to accelerators for critical training tasks.</span></p> </li> <li><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">ML and network co-design:</strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> The network is built in lockstep with each new generation of ML accelerators, helping ensure the fabric is matched to the hardware it supports.</span></li> </ol></div> <div class="block-image_full_width"> <div class="article-module h-c-page"> <div class="h-c-grid"> <figure class="article-image--large h-c-grid__col h-c-grid__col--6 h-c-grid__col--offset-3 " > <img src="https://storage.googleapis.com/gweb-cloudblog-publish/images/2_Data_center_network_architecture.max-1000x1000.png" alt="2 Data center network architecture"> </a> <figcaption class="article-image__caption "><p data-block-key="s0df9">Figure 2: Data center network architecture</p></figcaption> </figure> </div> </div> </div> <div class="block-paragraph_advanced"><h3><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">Introducing Virgo Network: Megascale data center fabric</span></h3> <p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">Virgo Network is a scale-out fabric designed for the extreme requirements of modern AI workloads. Built on high-radix switches that reduce network layers by allowing more ports per switch, it employs a flat, two-layer non-blocking topology. Compared with traditional datacenter networks, this significantly reduces latency by minimizing network tiers. It features a multi-planar design with independent control domains to connect accelerators (figure 3). The accelerator racks also connect with the Jupiter north-south fabric to access compute and storage services. Together, this streamlined architecture delivers the massive bisection bandwidth and deterministic low latency necessary for both distributed training and serving workloads.</span></p></div> <div class="block-image_full_width"> <div class="article-module h-c-page"> <div class="h-c-grid"> <figure class="article-image--large h-c-grid__col h-c-grid__col--6 h-c-grid__col--offset-3 " > <img src="https://storage.googleapis.com/gweb-cloudblog-publish/images/3_Megascale_data_center_fabric_Virgo_Netwo.max-1000x1000.png" alt="3 Megascale data center fabric (Virgo Network)"> </a> <figcaption class="article-image__caption "><p data-block-key="s0df9">Figure 3: Megascale data center fabric (Virgo Network)</p></figcaption> </figure> </div> </div> </div> <div class="block-paragraph_advanced"><p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">Virgo Network is the foundation of our next-generation accelerator designs and delivers the following advantages:</span></p> <ul> <li role="presentation"><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Massive fabric scale</strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">: </span><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">Virgo Network can link 134,000 chips (TPU 8t) with up to 47 petabits/sec of non-blocking bi-sectional bandwidth in a single fabric.</span><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> </span></li> <li role="presentation"><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Generational performance leap</strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">: With up to 4x the bandwidth per accelerator (TPU 8t) over the previous generation, Virgo Network delivers the bandwidth you need to get the full power of every chip. </span></li> <li role="presentation"><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Predictable low latency</strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">: Virgo Network delivers 40% lower unloaded fabric latency for TPUs compared to previous generation leading to more predictable performance for latency sensitive AI workloads.</span></li> </ul> <h3><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">Improving reliability at scale</span></h3> <p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">In a system supporting hundreds of thousands of chips, hardware failures are inevitable. Because a single faulty component can disrupt a synchronized training job, reliability at scale is a primary focus. To maximize workload goodput, we designed the Virgo Network architecture around fault isolation, deep observability, and the rapid mitigation of hangs and stragglers.</span></p> <p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">At this scale, system-wide resilience requires a solid network foundation. Virgo Network integrates independent switching planes that provide robust fault isolation, protecting cluster-wide goodput from being degraded by localized hardware failures.</span></p></div> <div class="block-image_full_width"> <div class="article-module h-c-page"> <div class="h-c-grid"> <figure class="article-image--large h-c-grid__col h-c-grid__col--6 h-c-grid__col--offset-3 " > <img src="https://storage.googleapis.com/gweb-cloudblog-publish/images/4_How_fail-stop_and_fail-slow_impact_MTTR.max-1000x1000.png" alt="4 How fail-stop and fail-slow impact MTTR"> </a> <figcaption class="article-image__caption "><p data-block-key="s0df9">Figure 4: How fail-stop and fail-slow impact MTTR</p></figcaption> </figure> </div> </div> </div> <div class="block-paragraph_advanced"><p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">Building on this foundation, we optimize the software and orchestration stack to maximize mean-time between interruptions (MTBI) and minimize mean-time to recovery (MTTR) through two primary areas:</span></p> <ul> <li aria-level="1" style="list-style-type: disc; vertical-align: baseline;"> <p role="presentation"><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Observability:</strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> Reliability at scale requires high-fidelity visibility. We use sub-millisecond telemetry to monitor network systems. This deep visibility allows us to detect transient congestion, optimize buffer management, and pinpoint the root causes of slowdowns across the hardware and software stack.</span></p> </li> <li aria-level="1" style="list-style-type: disc; vertical-align: baseline;"> <p role="presentation"><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Identifying stragglers and hangs:</strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> Proactive monitoring is critical for identifying nodes that are experiencing performance degradation (stragglers) or that have stopped responding completely (hangs). By rapidly localizing these bottlenecks, with automated </span><a href="https://cloud.google.com/blog/products/compute/stragglers-in-ai-a-guide-to-automated-straggler-detection?e=48754805"><span style="text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">straggler</span></a><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> and newly added hang detection, we accelerate the training job and protect it from localized slowdowns.</span></p> </li> </ul> <h3><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">The foundation of the AI Hypercomputer</span></h3> <p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">Virgo Network is a reimagined scale-out data center network custom-built for the stringent demands of modern AI workloads. This flat, multi-planar architecture unifies accelerators across pods into a single compute domain, addressing the bandwidth and scale limitations of traditional networks. By providing robust fault isolation directly at the hardware level, Virgo Network serves as the foundation for system-wide resilience, protecting synchronized workloads from localized hardware faults. </span></p> <p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">Ultimately, Virgo Network delivers the scale, predictable latency, and reliability necessary to accelerate the agentic AI era. To learn more about how we are building infrastructure for the future of AI, visit our</span><a href="https://cloud.google.com/ai-infrastructure"><span style="text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;"> AI infrastructure solutions page</span></a><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">, explore the </span><a href="https://docs.cloud.google.com/architecture/ai-ml"><span style="text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">technical documentation</span></a><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">, or attend the dedicated breakout </span><a href="https://www.googlecloudevents.com/next-vegas/session-library?session_id=3913087&amp;name=how-google&amp;" rel="noopener" target="_blank"><span style="text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">session</span></a><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> at Google Cloud Next.</span></p></div>Wed, 22 Apr 2026 12:00:00 +0000https://cloud.google.com/blog/products/networking/introducing-virgo-megascale-data-center-fabric/InfrastructureAI & Machine LearningGoogle Cloud NextSystemsNetworkingarticleIntroducing Virgo Network, Google’s scale-out AI data center fabrichttps://storage.googleapis.com/gweb-cloudblog-publish/images/GCN26_102_BlogHeader_2436x1200_Opt_2_Dark.max-600x600.jpgGooglehttps://cloud.google.com/blog/products/networking/introducing-virgo-megascale-data-center-fabric/Benny Siman-TovSenior Director Product ManagementArjun SinghEngineering FellowIntroducing Gemini Enterprise Agent Platform, powering the next wave of agentshttps://cloud.google.com/blog/products/ai-machine-learning/introducing-gemini-enterprise-agent-platform/<div class="block-paragraph_advanced"><p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">In the early days of generative AI, building safe and reliable business tools took massive engineering effort and a high tolerance for trial and error. We helped solve that with </span><span style="text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">Vertex AI</span><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">, our trusted AI development platform. But today, we’re managing a different level of complexity, with agents interacting across multiple systems — and often without security and governance guardrails. </span></p> <p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">To move toward a truly autonomous enterprise, one where agents can act with the same independence and reliability as a member of your team, you need a foundation that can sustain that level of trust. </span></p> <p><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">What’s new: </strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">Today, we’re launching </span><a href="https://console.cloud.google.com/agent-platform/overview"><span style="text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">Gemini Enterprise Agent Platform</span></a><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> — our new, comprehensive platform to build, scale, govern, and optimize agents. It’s the evolution of Vertex AI, bringing the model selection, model building, and agent building capabilities that customers love, together with new features for agent integration, DevOps, orchestration, and security. </span></p> <p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">Agent Platform provides a single destination for your technical teams to build agents that can transform your products, services, and operations. These agents can be seamlessly delivered to your employees through the </span><a href="https://cloud.google.com/blog/products/ai-machine-learning/whats-new-in-gemini-enterprise"><span style="text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">Gemini Enterprise app</span></a><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">, all while remaining tightly integrated with your IT operations to help ensure control, governance, and security as you scale.</span></p> <p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">The platform also provides first-class access to more than 200 of the world’s leading models through Model Garden. This includes our latest first-party breakthroughs like </span><a href="https://deepmind.google/models/gemini/pro/" rel="noopener" target="_blank"><span style="text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">Gemini 3.1 Pro</span></a><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">, </span><a href="https://deepmind.google/models/gemini-image/flash/" rel="noopener" target="_blank"><span style="text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">Gemini 3.1 Flash Image</span></a><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">, and </span><a href="https://deepmind.google/models/lyria/" rel="noopener" target="_blank"><span style="text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">Lyria 3</span></a><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">, alongside our open models like </span><a href="https://deepmind.google/models/gemma/gemma-4/" rel="noopener" target="_blank"><span style="text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">Gemma 4</span></a><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">. And, of course, customers have full flexibility to use the best model for the job with support for third-party models like Anthropic’s Claude Opus, Sonnet and Haiku. </span></p> <p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">Moving forward, all Vertex AI services and roadmap evolutions will be delivered exclusively through the Agent Platform, rather than as a standalone service, to power the next generation of agent development.</span></p> <p><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Why Agent Platform matters for your business: </strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">Agent Platform helps you move from managing individual AI tasks to delegating business outcomes with total confidence. You can: </span></p> <ul> <li aria-level="1" style="list-style-type: disc; vertical-align: baseline;"> <p role="presentation"><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Build:</strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> Choose the right environment for the job — from the low-code, visual interface of the new </span><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Agent Studio,</strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> to the code-first logic of the upgraded </span><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Agent Development Kit (ADK)</strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">. We’ve simplified the entire lifecycle with AI-native coding capabilities to help you ship production-grade agents faster.</span></p> </li> <li aria-level="1" style="list-style-type: disc; vertical-align: baseline;"> <p role="presentation"><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Scale:</strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> Clear the path to production with the re-engineered </span><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Agent Runtime</strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">. This supports long-running agents that maintain state for days at a time and are backed by </span><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Memory Bank</strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> for persistent, long-term context.</span></p> </li> <li aria-level="1" style="list-style-type: disc; vertical-align: baseline;"> <p role="presentation"><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Govern: </strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">Establish centralized control with </span><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Agent Identity, Agent Registry, and Agent Gateway</strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">. These capabilities help ensure every agent — whether built on Agent Platform or sourced from our partner ecosystem — has a trackable identity and operates within enterprise-grade guardrails. </span></p> </li> <li><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Optimize:</strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> Guarantee quality with </span><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Agent Simulation, Agent Evaluation, </strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">and</span><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;"> Agent Observability</strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">. These tools provide full execution traces and a real-time lens into agent reasoning to help ensure your agents always hit their goals.</span></li> </ul></div> <div class="block-image_full_width"> <div class="article-module h-c-page"> <div class="h-c-grid"> <figure class="article-image--large h-c-grid__col h-c-grid__col--6 h-c-grid__col--offset-3 " > <img src="https://storage.googleapis.com/gweb-cloudblog-publish/images/1_0_gemini_enterprise_agent_platform.max-1000x1000.jpg" alt="1 gemini enterprise agent platform"> </a> </figure> </div> </div> </div> <div class="block-paragraph_advanced"><p><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Get started with Agent Platform: </strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">Visit </span><a href="https://console.cloud.google.com/agent-platform/overview"><span style="text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">Agent Platform</span></a><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> in the Google Cloud console to explore new features and start building today. </span></p> <p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">Keep reading for a deeper look at our latest releases and how Agent Platform helps you deliver the production-ready agents you can trust at every stage of the journey.</span></p> <h3><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">How customers are achieving more with Gemini Enterprise Agent Platform</span></h3></div> <div class="block-image_full_width"> <div class="article-module h-c-page"> <div class="h-c-grid"> <figure class="article-image--large h-c-grid__col h-c-grid__col--6 h-c-grid__col--offset-3 " > <img src="https://storage.googleapis.com/gweb-cloudblog-publish/images/3_gemini_enterprise_agent_platform.max-1000x1000.jpg" alt="2- GEAP Logo Wall"> </a> </figure> </div> </div> </div> <div class="block-paragraph_advanced"><p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">"Burns &amp; McDonnell uses Agent Platform to transform how organizational knowledge is applied across the enterprise.
