Unlock more powerful reasoning by organizing agents into a network of sub-agents. This new, graph-based framework allows you to define clear, reliable logic for how agents work together to solve complex problems.</span></p> </li> <li aria-level="1" style="list-style-type: disc; vertical-align: baseline;"> <p role="presentation"><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Workspaces are secure-by-design: </strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">Give agents a hardened, sandboxed environment to run bash commands and manage files safely, isolated from your core systems.</span></p> </li> <li aria-level="1" style="list-style-type: disc; vertical-align: baseline;"> <p role="presentation"><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Multimodal streaming:</strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> Bring human-like stability to real-time interactions with multimodal support for live audio and video cues.</span></p> </li> </ul> <p><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Connect your agents to the enterprise</strong></p> <ul> <li aria-level="1" style="list-style-type: disc; vertical-align: baseline;"> <p role="presentation"><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Securely access any system:</strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> Use plug-and-play architecture with Native Ecosystem Integrations to connect agents to your internal data and tools without custom coding.</span></p> </li> <li aria-level="1" style="list-style-type: disc; vertical-align: baseline;"> <p role="presentation"><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Automate background operations:</strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> Activate your data in BigQuery and Pub/Sub with Batch &amp; Event-driven agents. This way, you can run massive, asynchronous tasks like content evaluation or data analysis in the background.</span></p> </li> </ul> <p><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Go from idea to production in hours</strong></p> <ul> <li aria-level="1" style="list-style-type: disc; vertical-align: baseline;"> <p role="presentation"><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Enable AI-driven development: </strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">A programmatic interface for coding agents to access Google’s complete suite of agentic capabilities, allowing them to build, evaluate, and deploy production-ready agents on your behalf.</span><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;"> </strong></p> </li> <li aria-level="1" style="list-style-type: disc; vertical-align: baseline;"> <p role="presentation"><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Bringing agent building directly to Agent Studio:</strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> Now, you can move seamlessly from building simple prompts to deploying complex agents in </span><a href="https://docs.cloud.google.com/gemini-enterprise-agent-platform/agent-studio/overview"><span style="text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">Agent Studio</span></a><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">. Once you're ready for deep customization, export your logic directly into ADK to continue development in a full-code environment.</span></p> </li> <li aria-level="1" style="list-style-type: disc; vertical-align: baseline;"> <p role="presentation"><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Get a head start with pre-built agents: </strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">Access a curated set of agent templates in </span><a href="https://docs.cloud.google.com/gemini-enterprise-agent-platform/build/agent-garden"><span style="text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">Agent Garden</span></a><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> — including code modernization, financial analysis, economic research, invoice processing, and more — that serve as immediate building blocks for your multi-agent systems.</span></p> </li> </ul> <h3><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">Scale AI agents</span></h3> <p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">To move from a proof-of-concept to a live environment, you need a platform that can handle the performance, state, and security requirements of real-world work. </span></p> <p><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Powering high-performance agent execution</strong></p> <ul> <li aria-level="1" style="list-style-type: disc; vertical-align: baseline;"> <p role="presentation"><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">The latest Agent Runtime: </strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">Our revamped </span><a href="https://docs.cloud.google.com/gemini-enterprise-agent-platform/build/runtime"><span style="text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">Agent Runtime</span></a><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> delivers sub-second cold starts and allows you to provision new agents in seconds.</span></p> </li> <li aria-level="1" style="list-style-type: disc; vertical-align: baseline;"> <p role="presentation"><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Support for multi-day workflows:</strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> You can now deploy long-running agents that run autonomously for days at a time. This allows your agents to manage complex, multi-step workflows and deep reasoning tasks that require extended persistence, like managing a sales prospecting sequence. </span></p> </li> <li aria-level="1" style="list-style-type: disc; vertical-align: baseline;"> <p role="presentation"><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Autonomous action with security-by-design environments:</strong><a href="https://docs.cloud.google.com/gemini-enterprise-agent-platform/scale/sandboxes"><span style="text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;"> </span></a><a href="https://docs.cloud.google.com/gemini-enterprise-agent-platform/scale/sandbox/code-execution-overview"><span style="text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">Agent Sandbox</span></a><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> </span><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">provides a hardened environment to safely execute model-generated code and perform computer use tasks like browser-based automation without risk to your host systems.</span></p> </li> <li aria-level="1" style="list-style-type: disc; vertical-align: baseline;"> <p role="presentation"><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Agent-to-agent orchestration:</strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> Enables agents to seamlessly delegate tasks to one another, including support for complex, generative, and deterministic orchestration patterns. This ensures that for critical flows such as compliance, your agents follow well-specified paths every time.</span></p> </li> </ul> <p><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Move beyond temporary session data to high-accuracy context</strong></p> <ul> <li role="presentation"><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Personalize interactions:</strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> </span><a href="https://docs.cloud.google.com/gemini-enterprise-agent-platform/scale/memory-bank"><span style="text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">Agent Memory Bank</span></a><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> dynamically generates and curates long-term memories from conversations. Using new Memory Profiles, agents can recall high-accuracy details with low latency, ensuring context is never lost.</span></li> <li role="presentation"><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Link AI interactions to your existing records: </strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">Store and manage history using </span><a href="https://docs.cloud.google.com/gemini-enterprise-agent-platform/scale/sessions"><span style="text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">Agent Sessions</span></a><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">. With Custom Session IDs, you can use your own unique identifiers to track sessions and map them directly to your internal database and CRM records.</span></li> <li aria-level="1" style="list-style-type: disc; vertical-align: baseline;"> <p role="presentation"><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Enable real-time, human-like interactions:</strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> Using the WebSocket protocol for Bidirectional Streaming, you can help ensure your agents are highly responsive during live customer or employee interactions, processing audio and video without lag.</span></p> </li> </ul> <h3><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">Govern AI agents</span></h3> <p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">Govern with a secure-by-design architecture that applies enterprise rigor to every agent in your fleet – from the ones you build on Agent Platform to the ones you source from our partner ecosystem.</span></p> <p><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Manage all of your agents through a single source of truth for identity and access.</strong></p> <ul> <li role="presentation"><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Assign every agent a verifiable identity: </strong><a href="https://docs.cloud.google.com/gemini-enterprise-agent-platform/scale/runtime/agent-identity"><span style="text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">Agent Identity</span></a><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> improves the security posture of your agents by ensuring every agent receives a unique cryptographic ID. This creates a clear, auditable trail for every action an agent takes, mapped back to defined </span><a href="https://docs.cloud.google.com/gemini-enterprise-agent-platform/scale/runtime/agent-identity"><span style="text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">authorization policies</span></a><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">.</span></li> <li aria-level="1" style="list-style-type: disc; vertical-align: baseline;"> <p role="presentation"><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Maintain a central library of approved tools:</strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> Our new <a href="https://docs.cloud.google.com/gemini-enterprise-agent-platform/govern/agent-registry"><span style="text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">Agent Registry</span></a></span><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> provides a single source of truth for your enterprise. It indexes every internal agent, tool, and skill, simplifying discovery and ensuring only governed, approved assets are available to your users.</span></p> </li> <li aria-level="1" style="list-style-type: disc; vertical-align: baseline;"> <p role="presentation"><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Manage your agent fleet from one control point:</strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> </span><a href="https://docs.cloud.google.com/gemini-enterprise-agent-platform/govern/gateways/agent-gateway-overview"><span style="text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">Agent Gateway</span></a><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> acts as the air traffic control for your agent ecosystem. It provides secure, unified connectivity between agents and tools across any environment, while enforcing consistent security policies and </span><a href="https://cloud.google.com/security/products/model-armor?e=48754805&amp;hl=en"><span style="text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">Model Armor</span></a><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> protections to safeguard against prompt injection and data leakage.</span></p> </li> </ul> <p><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Use AI-powered insights to detect hidden risks and suspicious behavior before they impact your business.</strong></p> <ul> <li role="presentation"><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Detect suspicious behavior in real-time:</strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> Agent Anomaly Detection uses statistical models and an LLM-as-a-judge framework to flag unusual reasoning. This works alongside </span><a href="https://docs.cloud.google.com/gemini-enterprise-agent-platform/govern/view-security-findings"><span style="text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">Agent Threat Detection</span></a><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;"> </strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">to provide visibility into malicious activity, such as reverse shells or connections to known bad IP addresses.</span></li> <li role="presentation"><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Uncover vulnerabilities automatically:</strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> A new </span><a href="https://docs.cloud.google.com/gemini-enterprise-agent-platform/govern/view-security-findings"><span style="text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">Agent Security</span></a><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> dashboard, powered by </span><a href="https://cloud.google.com/security/products/security-command-center"><span style="text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">Security Command Center</span></a><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">, unifies threat detection and risk analysis. It allows your teams to map relationships between agents and models, automate asset discovery, and scan for vulnerabilities in the underlying operating system and language packages.</span></li> </ul> <h3><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">Optimize AI agents </span></h3> <p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">Agent Platform gives you the visibility needed to understand how your AI is performing, making it easy to refine their logic and get smarter over time.</span></p> <p><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Test your agents before they ship</strong></p> <ul> <li role="presentation"><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Simulate realistic conversations: </strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">Use <a href="https://docs.cloud.google.com/gemini-enterprise-agent-platform/optimize/evaluation/evaluate-simulated"><span style="text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">Agent Simulation</span></a></span><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> to test agents against human-like synthetic user interactions and virtualized tools in a controlled environment. Agents are automatically scored based on task success and safety across multi-step conversations.</span></li> </ul> <p><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Monitor and improve in production</strong></p> <ul> <li role="presentation"><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Track live performance: </strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">Use </span><a href="https://docs.cloud.google.com/gemini-enterprise-agent-platform/optimize/evaluation/agent-evaluation"><span style="text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">Agent Evaluation</span></a><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> to continuously score agents against live traffic using multi-turn autoraters that can evaluate the logic of an entire conversation, not just a single response. With turnkey dashboards and </span><a href="https://docs.cloud.google.com/gemini-enterprise-agent-platform/optimize/observability/overview"><span style="text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">Agent Observability</span></a><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">, you can visually trace complex reasoning to debug issues as they happen.</span></li> <li role="presentation"><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Automate agent refinement: </strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">Instead of manually digging through logs, <a href="https://docs.cloud.google.com/gemini-enterprise-agent-platform/optimize/evaluation/optimize-agent"><span style="text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">Agent Optimizer</span></a> </span><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">automatically clusters real-world failures and suggests refined system instructions to improve accuracy.</span></li> </ul> <p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">Detailed technical guides and a full list of updates are available in our updated </span><a href="https://docs.cloud.google.com/gemini-enterprise-agent-platform"><strong style="text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">documentation</strong></a><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;"> </strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">and </span><a href="https://docs.cloud.google.com/gemini-enterprise-agent-platform/release-notes"><strong style="text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">release notes</strong></a><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">. </span><a href="http://cloud.google.com/products/gemini-enterprise-agent-platform"><span style="text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">Agent Platform </span></a><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">is the new standard for enterprise agent development, built to help you move from experimentation to production-scale impact, starting today.</span></p></div>Wed, 22 Apr 2026 12:00:00 +0000https://cloud.google.com/blog/products/ai-machine-learning/introducing-gemini-enterprise-agent-platform/Developers & PractitionersGoogle Cloud NextAI & Machine LearningarticleIntroducing Gemini Enterprise Agent Platform, powering the next wave of agentshttps://storage.googleapis.com/gweb-cloudblog-publish/images/0_gemini_enterprise_agent_platform.max-600x600.jpgGooglehttps://cloud.google.com/blog/products/ai-machine-learning/introducing-gemini-enterprise-agent-platform/Michael GerstenhaberVP, Product Management, Cloud AIMichael BachmanVP/GM, Cloud FoundationsNext ‘26: Redefining security for the AI era with Google Cloud and Wizhttps://cloud.google.com/blog/products/identity-security/next26-redefining-security-for-the-ai-era-with-google-cloud-and-wiz/<div class="block-aside"><dl> <dt>aside_block</dt> <dd>&lt;ListValue: [StructValue([(&#x27;title&#x27;, &#x27;Our news today from Next ‘26&#x27;), (&#x27;body&#x27;, &lt;wagtail.rich_text.RichText object at 0x7f8985fa6be0&gt;), (&#x27;btn_text&#x27;, &#x27;&#x27;), (&#x27;href&#x27;, &#x27;&#x27;), (&#x27;image&#x27;, None)])]&gt;</dd> </dl></div> <div class="block-paragraph_advanced"><p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">The AI era demands a new security era. Organizations are facing the dual challenge of harnessing the potential of AI while </span><a href="https://cloud.google.com/blog/topics/threat-intelligence/defending-enterprise-ai-vulnerabilities?e=48754805"><span style="text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">defending against its malicious use</span></a><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">, and Google Cloud can help you adapt and thrive.</span></p> <p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">The latest research from Google Cloud shows that adversaries are using AI to </span><a href="https://cloud.google.com/transform/new-mandiant-report-boost-basics-with-ai-to-counter-adversaries/"><span style="text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">accelerate the speed, scale, and sophistication of attacks</span></a><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">. Meanwhile, </span><a href="https://cloud.google.com/security/resources/m-trends?e=48754805"><span style="text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">M-Trends 2026</span></a><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> also showed that increased threat actor coordination has driven down the time to hand-off from an initial access to a secondary threat actor from eight hours to 22 seconds in the last three years.</span></p> <p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">Today at Google Cloud Next, we are showcasing how Google Cloud can help you defend against increasingly sophisticated threats at machine speed, protect AI and multicloud environments, and secure cloud workloads at scale. </span></p> <h3><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Delivering agentic defense </strong></h3> <p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">Our full-stack AI approach, from the chips to the models, gives you a competitive advantage with better integration and velocity to help protect customers. Not only can Google action insights from the world’s largest threat observatory and Mandiant frontline experts, but we also bring cutting-edge insights and breakthroughs from Google DeepMind, to help make your platforms more secure. </span></p> <p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">Today we are introducing three new agents in </span><a href="https://cloud.google.com/security/products/security-operations"><strong style="text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">Google Security Operations</strong></a><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> to help you defend at the speed of AI. </span></p> <ul> <li aria-level="1" style="list-style-type: disc; vertical-align: baseline;"> <p role="presentation"><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Threat Hunting agent</strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">, now in preview, can help teams proactively hunt for novel attack patterns and stealthy adversary behaviors that bypass traditional defenses. </span></p> </li> <li aria-level="1" style="list-style-type: disc; vertical-align: baseline;"> <p role="presentation"><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Detection Engineering agent</strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">, now in preview, can identify coverage gaps and create new detections for threat scenarios, reducing toil and transforming detection creation from a manual craft into an automated science. </span></p> </li> <li><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Third-Party Context agent, </strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">coming soon to preview, can enrich your workflows with contextual data from third-party content. </span></li> </ul></div> <div class="block-image_full_width"> <div class="article-module h-c-page"> <div class="h-c-grid"> <figure class="article-image--large h-c-grid__col h-c-grid__col--6 h-c-grid__col--offset-3 " > <img src="https://storage.googleapis.com/gweb-cloudblog-publish/original_images/1_-_Threat_Hunt_Initiation.gif" alt="1 - Threat Hunt Initiation"> </a> <figcaption class="article-image__caption "><p data-block-key="mhwgf">Initiating a threat hunt with the Threat Hunting agent</p></figcaption> </figure> </div> </div> </div> <div class="block-paragraph_advanced"><p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">Our </span><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Triage and Investigation agent</strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> processed over </span><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">5 million alerts</strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> in the last year, reducing a typical 30-minute manual analysis to 60 seconds with Gemini.</span><span style="text-decoration: line-through; vertical-align: baseline;"> </span></p> <p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">“Operational resilience and cybersecurity are the bedrock of customer trust at BBVA. By integrating advanced artificial intelligence, such as the Triage and Investigation agent, we are able to scale in new ways," said Diego Martinez Blanco, head of Security Technology, BBVA. </span></p> <p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">“It handles the initial heavy lifting and filters out false positives so we can prioritize issues that require human attention. The agent's transparent explanations allow our team to understand recommendations and ultimately dedicate our resources to more complex investigations,” he said.</span></p> <p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">You can build your own security agents with </span><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">remote Google Cloud model context protocol (MCP) server support for Google Security Operations</strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">, now generally available. To make it even easier, you can also access the MCP server client directly from the Google Security Operations chat interface, available in preview. </span></p></div> <div class="block-pull_quote"><div class="uni-pull-quote h-c-page"> <section class="h-c-grid"> <div class="uni-pull-quote__wrapper h-c-grid__col h-c-grid__col--8 h-c-grid__col-m--6 h-c-grid__col-l--6 h-c-grid__col--offset-2 h-c-grid__col-m--offset-3 h-c-grid__col-l--offset-3"> <div class="uni-pull-quote__inner-wrapper h-c-copy h-c-copy"> <q class="uni-pull-quote__text">Organizations leveraging an intelligence-led, AI-augmented approach to modern security operations with Google Cloud&#x27;s agentic defense can realize a strong ROI.</q> <cite class="uni-pull-quote__author"> <span class="uni-pull-quote__author-meta"> <strong class="h-u-font-weight-medium">Christopher Kissel</strong><br /> Research Vice President, IDC </span> </cite> </div> </div> </section> </div> </div> <div class="block-image_full_width"> <div class="article-module h-c-page"> <div class="h-c-grid"> <figure class="article-image--large h-c-grid__col h-c-grid__col--6 h-c-grid__col--offset-3 " > <img src="https://storage.googleapis.com/gweb-cloudblog-publish/original_images/2_-_Threat_Hunt_report.gif" alt="2 - Threat Hunt report"> </a> <figcaption class="article-image__caption "><p data-block-key="mhwgf">Findings report created by the Threat Hunting agent</p></figcaption> </figure> </div> </div> </div> <div class="block-paragraph_advanced"><p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">Security teams can also automate response actions with </span><a href="https://cloud.google.com/blog/products/identity-security/rsac-26-supercharging-agentic-ai-defense-with-frontline-threat-intelligence"><strong style="text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">agentic automation</strong></a><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> </span><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">in Google Security Operations. To further move teams from manual triage to agentic defense, we introduced </span><a href="https://cloud.google.com/blog/products/identity-security/bringing-dark-web-intelligence-into-the-ai-era"><strong style="text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">dark web intelligence</strong></a><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> in Google Threat Intelligence, now in preview. Internal tests show it can </span><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">analyze millions of daily external events with 98% accuracy</strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> to elevate threats that truly matter.</span></span></p> <p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">"IDC found that organizations experienced measurable operational gains, including substantial reductions in mean time to detect and mean time to respond, fewer false positives, and higher analyst productivity with AI-powered context and automation. These operational improvements translate into significant </span><a href="https://services.google.com/fh/files/misc/gti_idc_business_value_report.pdf" rel="noopener" target="_blank"><span style="text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">business outcomes</span></a><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">, such as shorter disruption periods, lower incident-related costs, and improved executive confidence in security posture and decision-making," said Christopher Kissel, research vice president, IDC. "Organizations leveraging an intelligence-led, AI-augmented approach to modern security operations with Google Cloud's agentic defense can realize a strong ROI." </span></p> <p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">New partner-supported workflows for Google Security Operations</strong></span></p> <p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">Today, we are also announcing a robust cohort of </span><a href="https://cloud.google.com/blog/products/identity-security/next26-announcing-new-partner-supported-workflows-for-google-security-operations"><span style="text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">new partner integrations</span></a><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> for Google Security Operations. Designed to deliver high-fidelity security workflows right out of the box, our latest participating Google Cloud Security integration ecosystem partners include Darktrace, Gigamon, and SAP.</span></p> <h3><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">Protecting AI and cloud applications across any infrastructure</span></h3> <p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">AI and cloud applications are built across multiple platforms and models. To protect them end-to-end, we want to make it easier and faster to mitigate risk, regardless of where and how you build. This support includes major cloud environments like Amazon Web Services, Google Cloud, Microsoft Azure, and Oracle Cloud; software-as-a-service (SaaS) environments like OpenAI; and even custom hosted environments. </span></p> <p><a href="https://cloud.google.com/blog/products/identity-security/google-completes-acquisition-of-wiz?e=48754805"><span style="text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">Wiz, now a part of Google Cloud</span></a><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">, expands and deepens our ability to protect the apps you build and run. Wiz empowers you to quickly and securely adopt AI, while also helping protect the AI development lifecycle. </span></p> <p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">Wiz announced its </span><a href="https://www.wiz.io/blog/introducing-wiz-ai-app" rel="noopener" target="_blank"><strong style="text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">AI-Application Protection Platform</strong></a><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> (AI-APP) at the RSA Conference, providing deep visibility, risk posture, and runtime analysis for your AI applications. Wiz also announced </span><a href="https://www.wiz.io/blog/introducing-wiz-agents" rel="noopener" target="_blank"><strong style="text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">Wiz Security Agents</strong></a><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> and </span><a href="https://www.wiz.io/blog/introducing-wiz-workflows" rel="noopener" target="_blank"><strong style="text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">Wiz Workflows</strong></a><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">, helping you identify and respond to risks and threats at machine speed.</span></p> <p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">Today, we’re taking our commitment to secure customers in any cloud, platform, and AI environment further. Wiz now </span><a href="https://www.wiz.io/blog/wiz-databricks-security-graph" rel="noopener" target="_blank"><span style="text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">supports Databricks</span></a><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> as well as new agent studios like AWS Agentcore, Gemini Enterprise Agent Platform, Microsoft Azure Copilot Studio, and Salesforce Agentforce, so customers gain visibility however their teams choose to build.</span></p> <p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">In addition, Wiz continues to support security ecosystems with integrations to the outer layer of the cloud, including </span><a href="http://wiz.io/blog/wiz-apigee-integration-for-api-discovery" rel="noopener" target="_blank"><span style="text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">Google Cloud Apigee</span></a><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">, </span><a href="https://www.cloudflare.com/press/press-releases/2026/cloudflare-partners-with-wiz-to-secure-the-global-ai-attack-surface/" rel="noopener" target="_blank"><span style="text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">Cloudflare AI Security for Apps</span></a><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">, and the </span><a href="https://www.wiz.io/blog/introducing-wiz-vercel-integration" rel="noopener" target="_blank"><span style="text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">Vercel platform</span></a><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">, further extending the power of the Wiz Security Graph. We’ve also updated how we integrate security detections from Wiz Defend with Google Security Operations and Mandiant Threat Defense to help analysts more easily configure automatic threat information forwarding.</span></p> <p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">Wiz is also announcing new capabilities designed to secure the AI-native development lifecycle, helping teams to innovate faster and more securely:  </span></p> <ul> <li aria-level="1" style="list-style-type: disc; vertical-align: baseline;"> <p role="presentation"><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Secure vibe-coded applications: </strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">Wiz is announcing a new integration, generally available in May, that runs Wiz security scanning directly inside the Lovable platform so vulnerabilities, secrets, and misconfigurations caught by Wiz surface in Lovable's built-in security view, right where teams are already building.</span></p> </li> <li aria-level="1" style="list-style-type: disc; vertical-align: baseline;"> <p role="presentation"><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Secure AI-generated code</strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">: </span><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">Wiz removes risks from AI-generated code the moment it is created. Inline AI security hooks integrate directly into IDEs and agent workflows to evaluate prompts and scan AI-generated output instantly, injecting security guardrails before the code is ever committed.</span></p> </li> <li aria-level="1" style="list-style-type: disc; vertical-align: baseline;"> <p role="presentation"><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Agent-based remediation</strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">: Wiz Skills equip coding agents and AI-native IDEs with full code-to-cloud context and validated attack surface findings from the Wiz Security Graph. These capabilities enable teams to trigger automated, agent-driven remediation workflows either locally from the developer's individual IDE or globally at the repository and pull request level within your version control system.</span></p> </li> <li aria-level="1" style="list-style-type: disc; vertical-align: baseline;"> <p role="presentation"><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Eliminate shadow AI</strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">: Wiz’s dynamic </span><a href="https://www.wiz.io/academy/ai-security/ai-bom-ai-bill-of-materials" rel="noopener" target="_blank"><span style="text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">AI-Bill of Materials</span></a><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> (AI-BOM)</span><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> automatically inventories all AI frameworks, models, and IDE extensions across your environment. This provides complete visibility into what is writing code across your stack, allowing you to track sanctioned corporate tools like Gemini Code Assist and GitHub Copilot while simultaneously uncovering unapproved shadow AI plugins.</span></p> </li> </ul> <p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">You can learn more about the </span><a href="https://wiz.io/blog/wiz-at-google-cloud-next" rel="noopener" target="_blank"><span style="text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">Wiz announcements here</span></a><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">.</span></p> <h3><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">Securing your agents and the agentic web</span></h3> <p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">In addition to securing your cloud and AI workloads, Google Cloud’s secure-by-design foundation can help you innovate at the speed of AI — from agents to fraud defense to the web.</span></p> <p><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Securing and governing agents with the Gemini Enterprise Agent Platform<br/></strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">To build, orchestrate, govern, and optimize agents</span><span style="font-style: italic; vertical-align: baseline;">, </span><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">today we are announcing </span><a href="https://cloud.google.com/blog/products/ai-machine-learning/introducing-gemini-enterprise-agent-platform"><strong style="text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">Gemini Enterprise Agent Platform</strong></a><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> including:</span></p> <ul> <li aria-level="1" style="list-style-type: disc; vertical-align: baseline;"> <p role="presentation"><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Agent Identity</strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> to enable access management and </span><a href="https://cloud.google.com/transform/these-4-ai-governance-tips-help-counter-shadow-agents"><span style="text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">AI governance at scale</span></a><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">. Our new</span><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;"> </strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">capability provides agents unique identities to operate autonomously with specific authentication flows, and with scoped human delegation.</span></p> </li> <li aria-level="1" style="list-style-type: disc; vertical-align: baseline;"> <p role="presentation"><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Agent Gateway, </strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">which</span><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;"> </strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">enables policy enforcement for all agent-to-agent and agent-to-tool connections. It governs your enterprise agent traffic and understands agent protocols like MCP and Agent2Agent (A2A) to inspect and secure every agent interaction.</span></p> </li> <li aria-level="1" style="list-style-type: disc; vertical-align: baseline;"> <p role="presentation"><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Model Armor</strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">,</span><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;"> </strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">our runtime protection for model and agent interactions, now integrates with Agent Gateway, </span><a href="https://docs.cloud.google.com/agent-builder/agent-engine/overview"><span style="text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">Agent Runtime</span><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">, and </span></a><a href="https://docs.cloud.google.com/model-armor/model-armor-langchain-integration"><span style="text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">Langchain</span></a><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> available in preview, and </span><a href="https://firebase.google.com/" rel="noopener" target="_blank"><span style="text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">Firebase</span></a><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">, generally available, to help developers add inline enforcement and sanitization of agent traffic and interactions without the need to change code. These integrations expand Model Armor's protection against runtime risks such as prompt injections, tool poisoning, and sensitive data leakage across </span><a href="https://docs.cloud.google.com/model-armor/integrations"><span style="text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">Google Cloud services and our AI portfolio</span></a><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">. </span></p> </li> </ul> <p><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Securing the agentic web with Google Cloud Fraud Defense and Chrome Enterprise<br/></strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">Today, we are evolving reCAPTCHA with the </span><a href="https://cloud.google.com/blog/products/identity-security/introducing-google-cloud-fraud-defense-the-next-evolution-of-recaptcha"><span style="text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">launch of </span><strong style="text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">Google Cloud Fraud Defense</strong></a><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">, generally available. This comprehensive platform is designed to discern the legitimacy and authorization of bots, humans, and agents. Using the same scale and signals that protect Google’s own ecosystem, Fraud Defense will soon offer in preview agent-specific capabilities for human users and AI agents that can help secure the digital commerce journey, from account creation and login to payment and checkout.</span></p> <p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">Our commitment to securing AI extends to the browser, a vital endpoint for interacting with AI. </span><a href="https://cloud.google.com/blog/products/chrome-enterprise/new-ways-to-navigate-the-ai-era-with-googles-enterprise-platforms-and-devices"><strong style="text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">Chrome Enterprise</strong></a><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> provides comprehensive data protection for the AI era with the visibility and controls needed to embrace AI safely without compromising corporate data:</span></p> <ul> <li aria-level="1" style="list-style-type: disc; vertical-align: baseline;"> <p role="presentation"><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">AI-aware extension threat detections</strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">, now in preview, can surface advanced extension telemetry that helps security teams detect and respond to anomalous AI agent activity. </span></p> </li> <li aria-level="1" style="list-style-type: disc; vertical-align: baseline;"> <p role="presentation"><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">New </span><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">shadow AI reporting</strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">, generally available soon, can help you gain visibility into the shadow AI landscape by flagging employee use of unsanctioned web-based AI and SaaS applications. </span></p> </li> </ul> <h3><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">What’s new in Trusted Cloud</strong></h3> <p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">We continue to offer new security controls and enhance capabilities across identity, data, and  networking on our cloud platform to help you secure your environments. Today we’re announcing the following updates:</span></p> <p><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Simplifying permissions with modern IAM<br/></strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">To help achieve least privilege quickly and simply, we’ve streamlined our predefined roles catalog with easy-to-use administrator, editor, and viewer roles, such as the </span><a href="https://docs.cloud.google.com/iam/docs/role-picker-gemini"><span style="text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">IAM role picker</span></a><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> and the ability to </span><a href="https://docs.cloud.google.com/docs/authentication/reauthentication"><span style="text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">re-authenticate sensitive actions</span></a><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">.</span></p> <p><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Data security<br/></strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">We are announcing several new capabilities for our cloud platform data security portfolio to help protect your most sensitive data and accelerate AI transformation.</span></p> <ul> <li aria-level="1" style="list-style-type: disc; vertical-align: baseline;"> <p role="presentation"><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Confidential Computing</strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">: In partnership with NVIDIA, today we’re announcing </span><a href="https://cloud.google.com/security/products/confidential-computing"><strong style="text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">Confidential Computing</strong></a><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;"> support for G4 VMs</strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">, featuring NVIDIA RTX PRO 6000 Blackwell Server Edition GPUs on Google Compute Engine (GCE) Confidential G4 VMs, available in preview globally, to help strengthen confidentiality and integrity for a wide spectrum of sensitive AI workloads. Coming soon in preview, SCC will automatically discover unmanaged agentic workloads — including agents, MCP servers hosted on Cloud Run, GKE, and inference endpoints running on GKE, and surface those as posture findings in SCC.</span></p> </li> <li aria-level="1" style="list-style-type: disc; vertical-align: baseline;"> <p role="presentation"><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">Our enhanced </span><a href="https://cloud.google.com/security/products/security-command-center?e=48754805"><span style="text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">Security Command Center Standard tier</span></a><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> provides data security posture management, compliance, vulnerability management, and risk analysis to help any Google Cloud customer establish strong security, compliance and risk coverage from the start at no additional costs. </span></p> </li> </ul> <h3><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">Take the next step</span></h3> <p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">When you make Google part of your security team, you gain the power of an intelligence-driven, AI-native defense; the freedom of an open cloud that’s secure-by-design; and the industry's most-battle tested experts as an extension of your organization. </span></p> <p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">For more on these new innovations and how you can secure what’s next, </span><a href="https://www.googlecloudevents.com/next-vegas/session-library?session_id=3818847&amp;name=secure-what&amp;" rel="noopener" target="_blank"><span style="text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">tune in to watch our security spotlight</span></a><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">.
