vertical-align: baseline;"> <p role="presentation"><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Scale the agentic task force with autonomy:</strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> Build and deploy long-running agents that independently solve complex problems up to days at a time, managed entirely through a new, unified Inbox command center.</span></p> </li> <li aria-level="1" style="list-style-type: disc; vertical-align: baseline;"> <p role="presentation"><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Collaborate with your colleagues and agentic task force in real-time:</strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> Transition from individual AI to collaborative, team-level productivity with Projects — a shared workspace for teams and agents—and the integrated Canvas editor.</span></p> </li> <li aria-level="1" style="list-style-type: disc; vertical-align: baseline;"> <p role="presentation"><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Govern with confidence with complete agent observability and traceability:</strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> The Gemini Enterprise app is built on our new Agent Platform, meaning enterprise-grade governance, observability, and granular control are built-in from day one.</span></p> </li> <li><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Connect your ecosystem:</strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> Orchestrate actions across Google Workspace, Microsoft 365, and a growing ecosystem of partner agents and data connectors.</span></li> </ul></div> <div class="block-image_full_width"> <div class="article-module h-c-page"> <div class="h-c-grid"> <figure class="article-image--large h-c-grid__col h-c-grid__col--6 h-c-grid__col--offset-3 " > <img src="https://storage.googleapis.com/gweb-cloudblog-publish/images/gemini_enterprise.max-1000x1000.jpg" alt="gemini enterprise"> </a> </figure> </div> </div> </div> <div class="block-paragraph_advanced"><h3><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Automate complex work with a digital taskforce</strong></h3> <p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">With our suite of agent building and management tools, anyone can manage a full spectrum of work — from immediate, ad-hoc tasks, to asynchronous, multi-step workflows that don’t require constant manual prompting.</span></p> <ul> <li><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Enhanced Agent Designer: </strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">Create an agent using natural language or a visual interface. Balance generative intelligence with deterministic nodes and flows that carry your business logic reliably. You can inspect, test, and approve every step of a workflow before it ever runs, ensuring enterprise transparency and trust. You can also seamlessly integrate human-in-the-loop checkpoints — ensuring your team can review actions, grant approvals, or provide expert guidance exactly when it matters most. These agents don’t just execute; they learn and improve with every human interaction.</span></li> </ul></div> <div class="block-image_full_width"> <div class="article-module h-c-page"> <div class="h-c-grid"> <figure class="article-image--large h-c-grid__col h-c-grid__col--6 h-c-grid__col--offset-3 " > <img src="https://storage.googleapis.com/gweb-cloudblog-publish/images/2_-Agent_Designer_1.max-1000x1000.png" alt="2 -Agent Designer (1)"> </a> </figure> </div> </div> </div> <div class="block-paragraph_advanced"><ul> <li><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Skills for reusable actions:</strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> </span><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">Codify your unique expertise into reusable Skills. Skills let you formalize a specific workflow — like applying brand guidelines or formatting a report — and save it as a reusable action for your whole team. Instead of re-explaining the context every time, the agent uses the appropriate skill automatically. Because our models dynamically load these Skills, your agents remain incredibly cost-efficient and laser-focused. They pull in deep expertise only when the task requires it, without cluttering the model’s reasoning.</span></li> </ul></div> <div class="block-image_full_width"> <div class="article-module h-c-page"> <div class="h-c-grid"> <figure class="article-image--large h-c-grid__col h-c-grid__col--6 h-c-grid__col--offset-3 " > <img src="https://storage.googleapis.com/gweb-cloudblog-publish/images/4-_Skills.max-1000x1000.png" alt="4- Skills"> </a> </figure> </div> </div> </div> <div class="block-paragraph_advanced"><ul> <li><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Long-running agents: </strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">Build and direct agents that can handle massive, multi-step workflows like end-to-end financial reconciliation or deep sales prospect sequencing, from ad hoc to recurring tasks. Operating autonomously from hours to days inside Google's secure cloud sandboxes, these agents orchestrate complex business logic in the background — powering through mission-critical work without requiring constant human supervision.</span></li> </ul></div> <div class="block-image_full_width"> <div class="article-module h-c-page"> <div class="h-c-grid"> <figure class="article-image--large h-c-grid__col h-c-grid__col--6 h-c-grid__col--offset-3 " > <img src="https://storage.googleapis.com/gweb-cloudblog-publish/images/3_-_Long_running_agents.max-1000x1000.png" alt="3 - Long running agents"> </a> </figure> </div> </div> </div> <div class="block-paragraph_advanced"><ul> <li><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Inbox for agent management:</strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> Inbox is a central command location to monitor, guide, and securely manage all of your agent activity. Notifications are intuitively categorized into actionable groups like "Needs your input," "Errors," and "Completed," giving you a clear, consolidated view of ongoing agent progress.</span></li> </ul></div> <div class="block-image_full_width"> <div class="article-module h-c-page"> <div class="h-c-grid"> <figure class="article-image--large h-c-grid__col h-c-grid__col--6 h-c-grid__col--offset-3 " > <img src="https://storage.googleapis.com/gweb-cloudblog-publish/images/5_-_Inbox.max-1000x1000.png" alt="5 - Inbox"> </a> </figure> </div> </div> </div> <div class="block-paragraph_advanced"><ul> <li><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Dynamic and interactive Agent UI experiences: </strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">Move beyond simple text chat. With new support for the Agent-to-UI protocol (A2UI), custom agents can dynamically generate rich, native UI components — like interactive data visualizations and structured forms — directly within the Gemini Enterprise app.</span></li> </ul></div> <div class="block-video"> <div class="article-module article-video "> <figure> <a class="h-c-video h-c-video--marquee" href="https://youtube.com/watch?v=j-Hnm4mkqgk" data-glue-modal-trigger="uni-modal-j-Hnm4mkqgk-" data-glue-modal-disabled-on-mobile="true"> <div class="article-video__aspect-image" style="background-image: url(https://storage.googleapis.com/gweb-cloudblog-publish/images/maxresdefault_ziYIfVV.max-1000x1000.jpg);"> <span class="h-u-visually-hidden">Dynamic and interactive Agent UI experiences in Gemini Enterprise</span> </div> <svg role="img" class="h-c-video__play h-c-icon h-c-icon--color-white"> <use xlink:href="#mi-youtube-icon"></use> </svg> </a> </figure> </div> <div class="h-c-modal--video" data-glue-modal="uni-modal-j-Hnm4mkqgk-" data-glue-modal-close-label="Close Dialog"> <a class="glue-yt-video" data-glue-yt-video-autoplay="true" data-glue-yt-video-height="99%" data-glue-yt-video-vid="j-Hnm4mkqgk" data-glue-yt-video-width="100%" href="https://youtube.com/watch?v=j-Hnm4mkqgk" ng-cloak> </a> </div> </div> <div class="block-paragraph_advanced"><ul> <li aria-level="1" style="list-style-type: disc; vertical-align: baseline;"> <p role="presentation"><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">High-code agents:</strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> Allow your engineering teams and IT leaders to build sophisticated agents with full code and publish them directly into the Gemini Enterprise app for the business to use.</span></p> </li> <li><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Data Insights agent for unified analysis:</strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> Data Insights is a native, out-of-the-box agent built by Google that uncovers deep patterns across your entire data landscape. By bridging structured data in warehouses and databases with the rich context of unstructured sources like docs, email, and chat, it provides a 360-degree view of your operations. The agent dynamically generates SQL and search queries to produce rich data visualizations — answering not just the “what,” but the critical “why” behind your business outcomes.</span></li> </ul></div> <div class="block-image_full_width"> <div class="article-module h-c-page"> <div class="h-c-grid"> <figure class="article-image--large h-c-grid__col h-c-grid__col--6 h-c-grid__col--offset-3 " > <img src="https://storage.googleapis.com/gweb-cloudblog-publish/original_images/6_-_Data_Insights_Agent.gif" alt="6 - Data Insights Agent"> </a> </figure> </div> </div> </div> <div class="block-paragraph_advanced"><ul> <li aria-level="1" style="list-style-type: disc; vertical-align: baseline;"> <p role="presentation"><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Enhanced Deep Research agent: </strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">Execute complex, multi-step research plans that autonomously synthesize information from the open web and internal company data. By combining iterative reasoning with long-running inference, the Deep Research agent can work in the background for hours to deliver comprehensive, citation-backed reports and executive summaries. </span></p> </li> </ul> <h3><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">Team productivity: Projects and Canvas</span></h3> <p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">Real work is a team sport. We are moving AI from a solo conversation to a persistent, shared team asset.</span></p> <ul> <li><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Projects:</strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> A dynamic, highly collaborative workspace where human experts and agents actively co-create side-by-side. By unifying your shared context across various sources — Google Workspace, Microsoft OneDrive, team chats, and more — the agent acts as a dedicated expert on your specific initiative. Whether your team is collaborating in real time or catching up asynchronously, you can work together to brainstorm new ideas, co-create key artifacts and make informed decisions that ultimately drive impactful outcomes, without ever having to sift through fragmented context.</span></li> </ul></div> <div class="block-image_full_width"> <div class="article-module h-c-page"> <div class="h-c-grid"> <figure class="article-image--large h-c-grid__col h-c-grid__col--6 h-c-grid__col--offset-3 " > <img src="https://storage.googleapis.com/gweb-cloudblog-publish/images/image5_7TbwtKM.max-1000x1000.png" alt="7 - Projects"> </a> </figure> </div> </div> </div> <div class="block-paragraph_advanced"><ul> <li><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Canvas: </strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">Stop tab-switching with an interactive editor built directly into Gemini Enterprise. Canvas allows teams to create and edit Docs or Slides in a single pane, with rich formatting and live co-editing. </span><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">We’ve also added Microsoft 365 interoperability, allowing you to export the docs and slides you've created within Canvas into common Microsoft Office formats. </span></li> </ul></div> <div class="block-image_full_width"> <div class="article-module h-c-page"> <div class="h-c-grid"> <figure class="article-image--large h-c-grid__col h-c-grid__col--6 h-c-grid__col--offset-3 " > <img src="https://storage.googleapis.com/gweb-cloudblog-publish/images/image10_2JqCMR8.max-1000x1000.png" alt="image10"> </a> </figure> </div> </div> </div> <div class="block-paragraph_advanced"><h3><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">An open and connected enterprise ecosystem</span></h3> <ul> <li><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">The enhanced Agent Gallery: </strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">Your Agent Gallery is the unified destination for every agent your teams need — whether built by Google, created internally by your company, or discovered through our partners. Today, we are launching Agent Marketplace integrated into the Agent Gallery, giving your users the ability to </span><a href="https://cloud.google.com/blog/products/ai-machine-learning/partner-built-agents-available-in-gemini-enterprise"><span style="text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">easily browse and request specialized third-party agents from partners like Accenture, Oracle, and ServiceNow</span></a><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">. Once approved, these agents seamlessly appear in the Agent Gallery, giving your team access to execute complex workflows with natural language right from within Gemini Enterprise.</span></li> </ul></div> <div class="block-image_full_width"> <div class="article-module h-c-page"> <div class="h-c-grid"> <figure class="article-image--large h-c-grid__col h-c-grid__col--6 h-c-grid__col--offset-3 " > <img src="https://storage.googleapis.com/gweb-cloudblog-publish/images/9_-_Agent_Gallery.max-1000x1000.png" alt="9 - Agent Gallery"> </a> </figure> </div> </div> </div> <div class="block-paragraph_advanced"><ul> <li aria-level="1" style="list-style-type: disc; vertical-align: baseline;"> <p role="presentation"><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Integrations for Bring Your Own Model Context Protocol (BYO-MCP):</strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> In addition to a rich set of rigorously validated, out-of-the-box connectors, we are introducing support for BYO-MCP. This allows admins to securely connect the Gemini Enterprise app directly to your own custom or third-party business tools, internal workflows, and custom-built applications. This capability expands your automation potential by allowing no-code agents to discover and execute tools hosted on your own servers — tailoring the AI experience to your specific enterprise workflows.</span></p> </li> <li aria-level="1" style="list-style-type: disc; vertical-align: baseline;"> <p role="presentation"><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Cross-platform unified intelligence: </strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">Gemini Enterprise delivers unified intelligence across your entire fragmented data landscape. Whether your data lives in Google Workspace, Microsoft 365, or other business applications, Gemini Enterprise strictly respects native permissions — ensuring your teams get powerful insights without ever compromising your company's governance or user access controls. </span></p> </li> </ul> <h3><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Enterprise-scale governance comes standard without additional cost</strong></h3> <p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">Confidence in enterprise AI is built on layers of trust. The Gemini Enterprise portfolio provides it at every level – without added cost. The entire system is built on Google’s secure-by-design infrastructure, with Agent Platform at its core providing access to universal governance controls. Any agent built on both Agent Platform and the Gemini Enterprise app is governed by the same universal rules, giving businesses a deeply integrated way to help secure agentic work. </span></p> <p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">Key controls now include:</span></p> <ul> <li aria-level="1" style="list-style-type: disc; vertical-align: baseline;"> <p role="presentation"><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Enforce granular access controls: </strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">Agent Identity lets you assign unique digital IDs and help enforce the principle of least privilege for every agent no matter where it runs. </span></p> </li> <li aria-level="1" style="list-style-type: disc; vertical-align: baseline;"> <p role="presentation"><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">Organize and share approved agents: Agent Registry gives IT teams a central catalog to curate and distribute approved, reusable agents for their employees. </span></p> </li> <li><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Turn “Shadow AI” into “Managed AI”: </strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">Agent Gateway gives IT teams a centralized management point for network policies, data access, and security guardrails — protecting against risks like prompt injection. Powered by our Context Aware Access capabilities, the Gateway enforces your company-specific rules and ensures agents never send data to unapproved endpoints.</span></li> </ul></div> <div class="block-image_full_width"> <div class="article-module h-c-page"> <div class="h-c-grid"> <figure class="article-image--large h-c-grid__col h-c-grid__col--6 h-c-grid__col--offset-3 " > <img src="https://storage.googleapis.com/gweb-cloudblog-publish/images/10_-_Gateway_Security_Page.max-1000x1000.jpg" alt="10 - Gateway Security Page"> </a> </figure> </div> </div> </div> <div class="block-paragraph_advanced"><p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">Learn more about Gemini Enterprise Agent Platform</span> <a href="https://cloud.google.com/blog/products/ai-machine-learning/introducing-gemini-enterprise-agent-platform"><span style="text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">here</span></a><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">.</span><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> </span></p> <p><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Availability</strong></p> <p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">New features will roll out to customers over the coming months. Ready to explore these new features and empower your teams? </span><a href="https://cloud.google.com/gemini-enterprise"><span style="text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">Get started with Gemini Enterprise today</span><span style="text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">.</span></a></p> <p> </p></div>Wed, 22 Apr 2026 12:00:00 +0000https://cloud.google.com/blog/products/ai-machine-learning/whats-new-in-gemini-enterprise/Google Cloud NextAI & Machine LearningarticleGemini Enterprise for the agentic task force: introducing long-running agents, agentic collaboration spaces, advanced governance, and morehttps://storage.googleapis.com/gweb-cloudblog-publish/original_images/gemini_enterprise_app_Q0nAHYn.jpgGooglehttps://cloud.google.com/blog/products/ai-machine-learning/whats-new-in-gemini-enterprise/Maryam GholamiSenior Director of Product, Gemini EnterpriseWhat’s next in Google AI infrastructure: Scaling for the agentic erahttps://cloud.google.com/blog/products/compute/ai-infrastructure-at-next26/<div class="block-paragraph_advanced"><p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">AI is evolving from answering questions to reasoning and taking action. Companies who want to lead in today’s agentic era require computing infrastructure designed and optimized for these new requirements. Today at Google Cloud Next, we are introducing new AI infrastructure capabilities that help you innovate faster, deliver compelling user and customer experiences, and optimize for cost and energy efficiency — all at massive scale. </span></p> <h3><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">The shift to agentic intelligence</span></h3> <p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">In the agentic era, a single intent triggers a chain reaction. Unlike chat, a primary AI agent decomposes goals into specific tasks for a fleet of specialized agents that then collaborate, preserve state, and use reinforcement learning to deliver outcomes in real-time. </span></p> <p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">This process scales intelligence per interaction, but also creates complexity that yesterday’s architectures cannot support without spiraling costs or performance bottlenecks. To scale efficiently and effectively, you must move beyond manually integrating fragmented components and technologies. To deliver agentic experiences that are smart, fast, scalable, and cost-effective, you need a unified infrastructure stack that spans purpose-built hardware, open software, and flexible consumption models.</span></p> <p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">Google’s </span><a href="https://cloud.google.com/solutions/ai-hypercomputer?e=48754805"><span style="text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">AI Hypercomputer</span></a><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> is AI-optimized infrastructure built for the agentic era, engineered to deliver on these new requirements. This is the same foundation that powers Google’s flagship Gemini models, consumer AI services, and enterprise AI offerings. Today, we are announcing a significant expansion of our AI infrastructure portfolio, including:</span></p> <ul> <li aria-level="1" style="list-style-type: disc; vertical-align: baseline;"> <p role="presentation"><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">TPU 8t and TPU 8i, </strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">our eighth generation TPUs </span></p> </li> <li aria-level="1" style="list-style-type: disc; vertical-align: baseline;"> <p role="presentation"><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">A5X bare metal instances,</strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> powered by NVIDIA Vera Rubin NVL72</span></p> </li> <li aria-level="1" style="list-style-type: disc; vertical-align: baseline;"> <p role="presentation"><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Axion N4A VMs,</strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> powered by our custom Axion Arm-based CPUs</span></p> </li> <li aria-level="1" style="list-style-type: disc; vertical-align: baseline;"> <p role="presentation"><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Google Compute Engine 4th generation VMs,</strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> powered by Intel and AMD x86-based CPUs</span></p> </li> <li aria-level="1" style="list-style-type: disc; vertical-align: baseline;"> <p role="presentation"><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Virgo Network, </strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">our breakthrough data center fabric for AI workloads</span></p> </li> <li aria-level="1" style="list-style-type: disc; vertical-align: baseline;"> <p role="presentation"><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Google Cloud Managed Lustre,</strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> a high-performance parallel file system</span></p> </li> <li aria-level="1" style="list-style-type: disc; vertical-align: baseline;"> <p role="presentation"><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Z4M VMs</strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> with high-capacity local SSD storage and RDMA for open parallel file systems</span></p> </li> <li aria-level="1" style="list-style-type: disc; vertical-align: baseline;"> <p role="presentation"><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Dedicated KV Cache</strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> scalable storage subsystem</span></p> </li> <li aria-level="1" style="list-style-type: disc; vertical-align: baseline;"> <p role="presentation"><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Native PyTorch</strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> support for TPUs</span></p> </li> <li aria-level="1" style="list-style-type: disc; vertical-align: baseline;"> <p role="presentation"><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">New Google Kubernetes Engine (GKE) capabilities</strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> for agent-native workload orchestration</span></p> </li> </ul></div> <div class="block-image_full_width"> <div class="article-module h-c-page"> <div class="h-c-grid"> <figure class="article-image--large h-c-grid__col h-c-grid__col--6 h-c-grid__col--offset-3 " > <img src="https://storage.googleapis.com/gweb-cloudblog-publish/images/1_ai_hypercomputer.max-1000x1000.png" alt="1 ai hypercomputer"> </a> </figure> </div> </div> </div> <div class="block-paragraph_advanced"><p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">Taken together, these capabilities will help you accelerate the development of models and complex agentic workflows to accelerate innovation, and deliver useful, responsive services to customers, all while reducing costs and using energy responsibly at scale.</span></p> <p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">Let’s take a closer look.</span></p> <h3><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">Introducing our eighth-generation TPU systems, purpose-built for agentic AI</span></h3> <p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">Today, we’re pleased to announce the </span><a href="https://blog.google/innovation-and-ai/infrastructure-and-cloud/google-cloud/eighth-generation-tpu-agentic-era" rel="noopener" target="_blank"><span style="text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">eighth generation of our Tensor Processing Units (TPUs)</span></a><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">, which for the first time includes two distinct chips and specialized systems, engineered specifically for the agentic era. </span></p> <p><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">TPU 8t </strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">is our training powerhouse, specifically designed for high-throughput AI workloads. It redefines the scale of AI development, delivering nearly 3x higher compute performance than previous generations to shrink training timelines for massive models. It packs 9,600 chips in a single superpod to provide 121 exaflops of compute and two petabytes of shared memory connected through high-speed inter-chip interconnects (ICI). This massive pool of compute, unified memory, and doubled ICI bandwidth helps ensure that even the most complex models achieve near-linear scaling and maximum system utilization. We can now turn months of training into weeks with the power of 1 million+ TPU chips in a single cluster, orchestrated by Pathways and JAX. </span></p> <p><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">TPU 8i</strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> is our breakthrough reasoning system for inference and reinforcement learning (RL), engineered to deliver the ultra-low latency required by agentic workflows and Mixture of Experts (MoE) models. By tripling on-chip SRAM to 384 MB and increasing high-bandwidth memory (HBM) to 288 GB, it breaks the memory wall, hosting massive KV Caches entirely on silicon. Additionally, it doubles ICI bandwidth to 19.2 Tb/s, reduces the ICI network diameter by over 50%, and introduces a dedicated Collectives Acceleration Engine (CAE), which reduces on-chip latency by up to 5x to minimize lag during high-concurrency requests. With this design, TPU 8i delivers 80% better performance per dollar for inference than the prior generation, enabling fast, interactive user experiences, cost-effectively.</span><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> </span></p> <p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">TPU 8t and TPU 8i will be available to Cloud customers soon. To learn more, check out this </span><a href="https://cloud.google.com/blog/products/compute/tpu-8t-and-tpu-8i-technical-deep-dive"><span style="text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">deep dive on the architecture</span></a><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">.</span></p> <h3><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">A5X with NVIDIA Vera Rubin platform</span></h3> <p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">We know that one size doesn't fit all. Different customers have different workloads, different requirements, and different use cases. So, we also partner deeply with NVIDIA to deliver the latest GPU platforms as highly reliable and scalable services in Google Cloud. We will be among the first to deliver instances based on the next-generation Vera Rubin platform when it becomes available later this year. </span></p> <p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">We are also co-engineering the open-source Falcon networking protocol with NVIDIA via the Open Compute Project, pushing the frontiers of reliable transport protocols. A5X will implement a variety of innovative concepts from Falcon.</span></p> <p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">Thinking Machine Labs, for example, uses our NVIDIA-based infrastructure to power Tinker, an open platform for reinforcement learning and fine-tuning of frontier models for specialized use cases, achieving over 2x faster training and serving with Google’s AI Hypercomputer.</span></p></div> <div class="block-paragraph_advanced"><h3><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">Fueling agentic logic and reinforcement learning with Axion, Intel, and AMD</span></h3> <p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">While GPUs and TPUs are great for training and serving AI models, they need to be complemented with high-performance CPU-based services to handle the complex logic, tool-calls, and feedback loops that surround the core AI model. Our </span><a href="https://cloud.google.com/blog/products/compute/whats-new-in-compute-at-next26"><span style="text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">new Axion-powered N4A CPU instances</span></a><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> deliver outstanding price-performance for these agent runtimes. In fact, GKE Agent Sandbox with Google Axion N4A offers up to 30% better price-performance than agent workloads on other hyperscalers. </span><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">This efficiency extends across our entire portfolio, including our 4th generation Compute Engine VM families, powered by the latest x86 instances from Intel and AMD. These are specifically optimized for the broadest range of RL tasks, such as RL reward calculation, agent orchestration, and nested visualization, providing the optimal capabilities for every AI workload. </span></p> <h3><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">Virgo Network for data center scale-out fabric</span></h3> <p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">As part of AI Hypercomputer, the </span><a href="https://cloud.google.com/blog/products/networking/introducing-virgo-megascale-data-center-fabric"><span style="text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">Virgo Network</span></a><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> is designed to meet the demanding requirements of modern large-scale AI workloads. Its collapsed fabric architecture with 4x the bandwidth of previous generations eliminates the "scaling tax" to deliver staggering peak computing power. This capacity helps the most ambitious AI workloads scale with near-linear efficiency.</span></p> <p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">With Virgo Network and TPU 8t, we can connect 134,000 TPUs into a single fabric in a single data center, and connect more than one million TPUs across multiple data center sites into a training cluster — essentially transforming globally distributed infrastructure into one seamless supercomputer. </span></p> <p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">We are also making Virgo Network available for A5X (powered by NVIDIA Vera Rubin NVL72), supporting up to 80,000 GPUs in a single data center, and up to 960,000 GPUs across multiple sites. </span></p> <h3><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">Storage: Minimizing data bottlenecks</span></h3> <p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">A massive compute cluster is only as effective as the storage system feeding it data. To ensure storage is not a bottleneck while making compute faster, we are delivering four key storage advancements that let you: </span></p> <ul> <li aria-level="1" style="list-style-type: disc; vertical-align: baseline;"> <p role="presentation"><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Accelerate training and inference: </strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">Google Cloud Managed Lustre now delivers 10 TB/s of bandwidth — a 10x improvement over last year and up to 20x faster than other hyperscalers. We’ve also increased its capacity to 80 petabytes. These advancements are powered by our new C4NX instances and Hyperdisk Exapools. </span></p> </li> <li aria-level="1" style="list-style-type: disc; vertical-align: baseline;"> <p role="presentation"><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Minimize latency:</strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> Managed Lustre can leverage new TPUDirect and RDMA to allow data to bypass the host, moving directly to the accelerators. By removing this processing overhead, your AI agents can respond with the near-instant speed users need. </span></p> </li> <li aria-level="1" style="list-style-type: disc; vertical-align: baseline;"> <p role="presentation"><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Maintain peak utilization for training:</strong><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;"> </strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">Rapid Buckets on Google Cloud Storage transforms object storage with sub-millisecond latency and 20 million operations per second. This helps ensure large-scale training checkpoints and recoveries happen near-instantly, allowing your accelerators to maintain 95% utilization or higher, accelerating training cycles, while also providing cost-effective utilization of valuable TPUs and GPUs.</span></p> </li> <li aria-level="1" style="list-style-type: disc; vertical-align: baseline;"> <p role="presentation"><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Build custom solutions:</strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> For ISVs and organizations that want to build storage solutions, we are launching the</span><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;"> </strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">Z4M instance, specifically engineered for customers who want to integrate trusted parallel file systems like Vast Data or Sycomp. Each Z4M instance scales to a massive 168 TiB of local SSD capacity and can be deployed in RDMA clusters of thousands of machines. </span></p> </li> </ul> <p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">These new storage options provide a comprehensive storage portfolio, giving you the raw power of the AI Hypercomputer stack with optimal storage services for each use-case.</span></p> <h3><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">GKE: Orchestration for agent-native workloads</span></h3> <p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">In the agentic era, intelligence is only as effective as the speed at which it can be scaled. So, we’ve transformed GKE to serve as the premier orchestration engine for agent-native workloads.</span></p> <p><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Reducing latency across the stack<br/></strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">To support responsive agentic responses, we optimize every millisecond of the start-up and scale-out process. By streamlining how infrastructure responds to surges in demand, GKE ensures that your agents are ready the moment a user engages with the system. New in GKE are:</span></p> <ul> <li aria-level="1" style="list-style-type: disc; vertical-align: baseline;"> <p role="presentation"><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Accelerated node and pod startup:</strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> GKE nodes now start up to 4x faster, while pod startup times have been slashed by up to 80%.</span></p> </li> <li aria-level="1" style="list-style-type: disc; vertical-align: baseline;"> <p role="presentation"><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Rapid model loading:</strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> Leveraging the run:AI Model Streamer and Rapid Cache in Google Cloud Storage, models now load 5x faster, removing a traditional storage bottleneck.</span></p> </li> </ul> <p><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Intelligent routing with AI-powered Inference Gateway<br/></strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">Building on last year's introduction of GKE Inference Gateway, we are using "AI for AI" to solve the complexities of serving at scale. </span></p> <p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">Inference Gateway’s new predictive latency boost replaces heuristic guesswork with machine learning-driven, real-time capacity-aware routing. This intelligent orchestration cuts time-to-first-token (TTFT) latency by more than 70% without manual tuning. For businesses, this translates directly into more natural voice conversations and smooth, real-time interactions across a range of use cases. </span></p> <p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">Inference Gateway can be deployed alongside llm-d, a Kubernetes-native high-performance distributed LLM inference framework, which was </span><a href="https://cloud.google.com/blog/products/containers-kubernetes/llm-d-officially-a-cncf-sandbox-project"><span style="text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">recently accepted</span></a><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> as a Cloud Native Computing Foundation (CNCF) Sandbox project. Google Cloud is proud to be a founding contributor to llm-d alongside Red Hat, IBM Research, CoreWeave, and NVIDIA, uniting around a clear, industry-defining vision: any model, any accelerator, any cloud. </span></p></div> <div class="block-image_full_width"> <div class="article-module h-c-page"> <div class="h-c-grid"> <figure class="article-image--large h-c-grid__col h-c-grid__col--6 h-c-grid__col--offset-3 " > <img src="https://storage.googleapis.com/gweb-cloudblog-publish/images/3_loveable_quote.max-1000x1000.png" alt="3 loveable quote"> </a> </figure> </div> </div> </div> <div class="block-paragraph_advanced"><h3><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">Open software ecosystem for the full AI lifecycle </span></h3> <p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">Hardware reaches its full potential through co-designed software. AI Hypercomputer enables engineers to move faster by providing native, optimized support for the industry’s most popular frameworks, including JAX, PyTorch, and vLLM. This open software layer reduces friction between development and deployment, translating to faster time-to-market and better resource efficiency.</span><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;"> </strong></p> <p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">We are now in preview with select customers with native PyTorch support for TPU, which we call TorchTPU. With TorchTPU, you can run models on TPUs as they are, with full support for native PyTorch features like Eager Mode. When you combine this with our robust support of vLLM on TPU, our message is clear: we always focus on building for openness and customer choice.</span></p> <h3><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">Your foundation for agentic growth</span></h3> <p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">To innovate quickly and cost-effectively in the agentic era, you need a unified system that doesn’t compromise on performance or choice. That is exactly what AI Hypercomputer delivers. By co-designing every layer — from the silicon to the software — we remove the integration burden so your teams can focus on driving your business forward. </span></p> <p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">AI Hypercomputer also serves as the powerful foundation for Google’s entire ecosystem of high-level services. Our </span><a href="https://cloud.google.com/blog/products/compute/google-cloud-ai-infrastructure-at-nvidia-gtc-2026"><span style="text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">longstanding partnership with NVIDIA</span></a><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> allows these startups to train and serve AI models, support fine-tuning, and scale new agentic workloads. </span></p> <p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">This week at Google Cloud Next, we’re highlighting the successes these customers are having and announcing exciting new partnerships with more startups choosing to utilize NVIDIA AI infrastructure and Google Cloud’s AI stack. </span></p> <p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">These new and expanding customers include:</span></p> <ul> <li aria-level="1" style="list-style-type: disc; vertical-align: baseline;"> <p role="presentation"><a href="https://thinkingmachines.ai/" rel="noopener" target="_blank"><strong style="text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">Thinking Machines Labs</strong></a><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> will utilize the latest NVIDIA Blackwell chips through Google Cloud, including being among the first Google Cloud customers to utilize GB300s. In early testing, Thinking Machines has seen training and serving speed increase 2x on GBs compared to prior generation chips. </span></p> </li> <li aria-level="1" style="list-style-type: disc; vertical-align: baseline;"> <p role="presentation"><a href="https://www.gmicloud.ai/en" rel="noopener" target="_blank"><strong style="text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">GMI Cloud</strong></a><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> leverages Google Cloud’s GPU infrastructure to run its inference-optimized platform, powering GMI Studio workflows and large-scale model serving across text, image, and video. Our deep partnership with NVIDIA means that the </span><a href="https://cloud.google.com/solutions/ai-hypercomputer?e=48754805"><span style="text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">Google Cloud AI Hypercomputer</span></a><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> is highly optimized for GPU customers and can deliver ultra-low latency, high-throughput, and cost-effective performance across multiple use cases.</span></p> <p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">Startups are choosing to utilize GPUs through Google Cloud in part because of this high level of optimization and because they can easily access highly differentiated technologies in our AI stack like </span><a href="https://cloud.google.com/gemini-enterprise"><span style="text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">Gemini Enterprise</span></a><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">, </span><a href="https://cloud.google.com/products/agent-builder"><span style="text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">Agent Builder</span></a><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">, BigQuery, Google Kubernetes Engine, and much more.</span></p> <p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">We also continue to partner closely with NVIDIA to support early-stage startups with AI compute and cloud services through </span><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">NVIDIA’s Inception program</strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> and our Google for Startups Cloud Program. If your startup is utilizing AI to build the next generation of security solutions, we invite you to apply to join us!</span></p> <h3><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Join the Google for Startups AI Agents Challenge</strong></h3> <p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">Startups, it's your chance to get hands-on right away. We’re excited to launch </span><a href="https://devpost.team/hackathon_guest_invites/4fb181b4-2722-415d-a442-285a57dcaba5?utm_source=linkedin&amp;utm_medium=social&amp;utm_campaign=google-for-startups-ai-agents-challenge&amp;utm_content=linkedin-post" rel="noopener" target="_blank"><span style="text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">the Google for Startups AI Agents Challenge</span></a><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> at Next 2026. </span></p> <p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">Open to anyone (not just Next attendees), this global competition runs for six weeks and gives teams $500 in credits and the tools — like the new Gemini Enterprise Agent Platform — to build autonomous systems and compete for a share of a $90,000 prize pool. </span></p> <p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">The challenge, which opens for submissions today, and runs until June 5, 2026, offers three tracks tailored to where you are in your development journey. You can build a net-new agent from scratch, optimize an existing prototype for production reliability, or refactor a business-ready agent for potential enterprise distribution on Google Cloud Marketplace and the Gemini Enterprise app.</span></p> <p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">Submissions will be evaluated based on the following weighted criteria: Technical Implementation (30%), Business Case (30%), Innovation and Creativity (20%), and Demo and Presentation (20%). </span><a href="https://devpost.team/hackathon_guest_invites/4fb181b4-2722-415d-a442-285a57dcaba5?utm_source=linkedin&amp;utm_medium=social&amp;utm_campaign=google-for-startups-ai-agents-challenge&amp;utm_content=linkedin-post" rel="noopener" target="_blank"><span style="text-decoration: underline; With 400 million SMBs worldwide and 36 million in the U.S. alone, they provide 50% of global employment. Now, with Google Cloud AI, they’re scaling faster, operating more efficiently, and delivering better results for their customers. </span></p> <p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">For years SMBs have been working with cutting edge products like Google Workspace, Google Ads, Search, YouTube, Maps, Google Wallet, and more to grow their business. Now, more SMBs are taking the first big steps in their AI journeys with our </span><a href="https://docs.cloud.google.com/vertex-ai/generative-ai/docs/models"><span style="text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">leading models</span></a><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> and our agentic platform, </span><a href="https://cloud.google.com/gemini-enterprise?utm_source=google&amp;utm_medium=cpc&amp;utm_campaign=1713762-Gemini_Enterprise-DR-NA-US-en-Google-BKWS-EXA-GEnterprise&amp;utm_content=c-Hybrid+%7C+BKWS+-+MIX+%7C+Txt_Gemini+Enterprise-189528400785&amp;utm_term=gemini+enterprise&amp;gclsrc=aw.ds&amp;gad_source=1&amp;gad_campaignid=23370621055&amp;gclid=CjwKCAjw-dfOBhAjEiwAq0RwI43PsghfiED_EbABt-WPxov8U-n63h1loBCX5IafOTKD6V3bFeuuRBoCaz4QAvD_BwE&amp;e=48754805"><span style="text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">Gemini Enterprise</span></a><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">. </span></p> <p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">By making AI accessible to every employee, Gemini Enterprise serves as a launchpad for SMBs ready to develop an AI strategy and build new solutions to work smarter than ever before.Businesses are using AI to automate manual tasks and build custom solutions that extend their reach and help them better support their own customers. </span></p> <p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">We are proud to support these early milestones, and at Next we’re excited to showcase </span><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">dozens of new customer partnerships</strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> with organizations taking their first steps toward an AI-driven future. This means faster, smarter resolutions, building upon the success thousands of customers are already seeing from Gemini within Agentforce to build prompts.</span></p> </li> <li aria-level="1" style="list-style-type: disc; vertical-align: baseline;"> <p role="presentation"><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">SAP </strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">is </span><a href="https://cloud.google.com/blog/topics/partners/sap-partnership-unified-data-foundation-zero-copy-sharing-agentic-business-engagement-cloud"><span style="text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">integrating</span></a><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> Gemini Enterprise into its Engagement Cloud to deliver AI-powered customer service and sales insights alongside creative tools for image and text generation.</span></p> </li> <li aria-level="1" style="list-style-type: disc; vertical-align: baseline;"> <p role="presentation"><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">ServiceNow</strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> is integrating its AI agents with Gemini Enterprise, bringing autonomous operations to the world’s largest enterprises</span></p> </li> </ul> <h3><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Building a partner channel for the agentic era</strong></h3> <p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">Our new partner program, </span><a href="https://partners.cloud.google.com/"><span style="text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">Google Cloud Partner Network</span></a><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">, is designed to help partners thrive in the agentic era. Last year, we used AI to unlock deep insights across our partner tools; now, we are building the agentic workflows that turn those insights into autonomous growth. Key updates include:</span></p> <ul> <li aria-level="1" style="list-style-type: disc; vertical-align: baseline;"> <p role="presentation"><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">The Partner Agent:</strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> Integrated into the Partner Network Hub, this agentic tool acts as a central orchestrator for the partner experience. Beyond answering questions, it actively guides partners on next steps, summarizes complex assets, and provides real-time coaching for registrations and statements of work.</span></p> </li> <li aria-level="1" style="list-style-type: disc; vertical-align: baseline;"> <p role="presentation"><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">The Agentic Earnings Hub:</strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> Here, partners can find new capabilities to auto-draft statements of work and monitor consumption milestones to auto-generate claim requests. When paired with the Earnings Potential Modeler, these tools provide contextual recommendations to map every available incentive down to the individual client level.</span></p> </li> <li aria-level="1" style="list-style-type: disc; vertical-align: baseline;"> <p role="presentation"><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Partner Finder:</strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> We are also extending this intelligence to customers, turning discovery into a conversational experience where natural language prompts pinpoint the ideal partners for the most hyper-specific workloads.</span></p> </li> </ul> <p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">Finally, we’re honored to highlight </span><a href="https://cloud.google.com/blog/topics/partners/2026-partners-of-the-year-winners-next26"><span style="text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">the winners of </span><strong style="text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">Google Cloud’s 2026 Partner Awards</strong></a><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">, which celebrate the transformative impact and incredible value our partners have delivered for customers over the past year. This update shifts your Google Cloud operations from manual workflows to a proactive, intelligent experience supported by a powerful ecosystem of agents.</span></p> <p><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Why it matters: </strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">A new agentic architecture enables Gemini Cloud Assist to handle the heavy lifting of your cloud management. By embedding intelligence, your enterprise context, and the power of Gemini directly into the operational layer, Gemini Cloud Assist proactively executes complex tasks such as designing applications, troubleshooting issues, and preemptively optimizing costs, that previously required constant human oversight. In enterprise-scale systems, this approach accelerates development velocity and reduces resolution times. </span></p> <p><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">What’s new: </strong></p> <ul> <li aria-level="1" style="list-style-type: disc; vertical-align: baseline;"> <p role="presentation"><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">Using natural language and the power of Gemini, reduce the time from design to deployment of new or existing multi-resource deployments via a </span><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">redesigned Application Design Center</strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">.</span></p> </li> <li aria-level="1" style="list-style-type: disc; vertical-align: baseline;"> <p role="presentation"><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">Automate infrastructure operations via </span><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">gcloud, kubectl, and Terraform </strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">while using proactive multi-turn agents to troubleshoot and resolve incidents.</span></p> </li> <li aria-level="1" style="list-style-type: disc; vertical-align: baseline;"> <p role="presentation"><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Identify your cost anomalies 24/7 </strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">using a proactive FinOps agent that analyzes spending spikes and generates granular cost reports on demand.</span></p> </li> <li aria-level="1" style="list-style-type: disc; vertical-align: baseline;"> <p role="presentation"><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Assistance wherever you are. </strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">Powered by </span><a href="https://docs.cloud.google.com/mcp/supported-products"><span style="text-decoration: underline; vertical-align: baseline;">Google Cloud MCP servers</span></a><span style="vertical-align: baseline;"> and our proactive agents under the hood, Gemini Cloud Assist also exposes its own design, operation, troubleshooting and optimization capabilities as published MCP servers, bringing them straight to your IDE. </span></p> </li> </ul> <p style="padding-left: 40px;"><span style="font-style: italic; vertical-align: baseline;">“Gemini Cloud Assist has significantly helped our dev teams. It reduced the number of outreach and touch points I have with them regarding Google Cloud questions by 60%. This allows our cloud team to scale more effectively and focus on more complex tasks.” </span><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">- Oscar Aldana Assad, Senior Cloud Engineer, Petco</span></p> <p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">Let’s take a deeper look at how the agentic Gemini Cloud Assist can help your operations.</span></p> <h3><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">Accelerate production-readiness with Application Design Center</span></h3> <p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">Gemini Cloud Assist serves as the intelligent reasoning engine for Application Design Center, acting as the bridge between natural-language intent, and a visual, production-ready architecture. By describing your infrastructure goals in plain language, Gemini Cloud Assist leverages Application Design Center to automatically lay out a visual design, including deployable Terraform. These templates are based on best-practice architecture guidance from Google Cloud and help bring security, reliability and compliance by design. Integrated with Security Command Center, quickly go from idea to deployment that conforms to your organizational policies.</span></p> <p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">Platform teams can then curate shared catalogs of pre-approved templates and integrate their own custom Terraform modules directly into the design process, providing a governed framework. This established, well-lit path helps developers adhere to organizational security and compliance guardrails from the first day of deployment. Beyond initial deployment, Gemini supports the full application lifecycle with interactive, multi-turn problem solving to update cloud resources. </span></p></div> <div class="block-paragraph_advanced"><h3><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">Move from reactive to proactive remediation</span></h3> <p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">In production, Gemini Cloud Assist helps you shift operations from reactive troubleshooting to quickly analyzing hypotheses to drive a lower time to resolution. Triggered by alerts, Gemini Cloud Assist proactively clusters and analyzes signals to initiate investigations before issues escalate. Now with Gemini 3, Gemini Cloud Assist correlates logs and metrics and identifies root causes from infrastructure signals down to the application code. Gemini Cloud Assist explores parallel hypotheses via tool calls and presents a technical breakdown of observations in a centralized UI. If intervention is required to address an underlying Google Cloud issue, users can hand off complete context to Google support, minimizing the iterations required for sharing configuration and context data.</span></p></div> <div class="block-image_full_width"> <div class="article-module h-c-page"> <div class="h-c-grid"> <figure class="article-image--large h-c-grid__col h-c-grid__col--6 h-c-grid__col--offset-3 " > <img src="https://storage.googleapis.com/gweb-cloudblog-publish/original_images/proactive_alert_investigations_blog.gif" alt="proactive_alert_investigations"> </a> </figure> </div> </div> </div> <div class="block-paragraph_advanced"><h3><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">Identify cost anomalies 24/7</span></h3> <p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">To maintain economic health, Gemini Cloud Assist now acts as an proactive optimization agent for your projects. Running in the background 24/7, it monitors for cost anomalies and provides root-cause analysis, correlating spending spikes with specific engineering triggers like new resource creation, auto-scaling events, or pricing changes. You can query resource utilization via natural language to generate on-demand, tabulated reports, by project and applications registered in AppHub, providing granular visibility into "</span><span style="font-style: italic; vertical-align: baseline;">who, what, when, and how</span><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">" — without manual data aggregation. For example, you can ask ‘Why did the cost of my application increase yesterday?’ or ‘How much did my project cost last month?’ and Gemini Cloud Assist answers by correlating cost data with infrastructure change, audit, and monitoring logs to get you an accurate answer.</span></p></div> <div class="block-image_full_width"> <div class="article-module h-c-page"> <div class="h-c-grid"> <figure class="article-image--large h-c-grid__col h-c-grid__col--6 h-c-grid__col--offset-3 " > <img src="https://storage.googleapis.com/gweb-cloudblog-publish/original_images/3_Vz6FwaI.gif" alt="3"> </a> </figure> </div> </div> </div> <div class="block-paragraph_advanced"><h3><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">Assistance everywhere</span></h3> <p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">We are meeting teams where they work by expanding the surfaces where Gemini Cloud Assist is available. A Gemini Cloud Assist agent is already accessible through the console and mobile interfaces. And with new support for the Model Context Protocol (MCP), Gemini Cloud Assist is now available in Gemini CLI, your favorite agentic IDE or CLI, and third-party toolchains like ServiceNow and Slack. Integrating proactive assistance within existing workflows helps teams to avoid context switching and maintain flow-state.</span></p> <h3><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">Proactive capabilities at your fingertips</span></h3> <p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">We designed Gemini Cloud Assist to help manage the end-to-end lifecycle of your applications, providing a multi-agent approach from deploying new applications to managing existing applications in the cloud. With the help of Gemini 3, Gemini Cloud Assist can now:</span></p> <ul> <li role="presentation"><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Increase your development velocity: </strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">Accelerate production-readiness using intent-driven architectures that unify best practices, security policies, and enterprise compliance.</span></li> <li role="presentation"><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Streamline production operations</strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">: Triage, diagnose and resolve production issues faster, through Gemini-based troubleshooting, recommendations and remediations.</span></li> <li role="presentation"><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Automate cost optimization:  </strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">Automatically detect, analyze, root-cause, and alert you about cost anomalies for your projects on a daily basis. </span></li> <li role="presentation"><strong style="vertical-align: baseline;">Meet your teams where they are:  </strong><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">Through proactive agents and MCP tools, engage with functionality using surfaces that range from the Google Cloud console to your CLI and IDE, so teams can stay in a flow-state.</span></li> </ul> <p><span style="vertical-align: baseline;">The future of operations is agentic.
